### How to use skills
- Discovery: The list above is the skills available in this session (name + description + file path). Skill bodies live on disk at the listed paths.
- Trigger rules: If the user names a skill (with $SkillName or plain text) OR the task clearly matches a skill's description shown above, you must use that skill for that turn. Multiple mentions mean use them all. Do not carry skills across turns unless re-mentioned.
- Missing/blocked: If a named skill isn't in the list or the path can't be read, say so briefly and continue with the best fallback.
- How to use a skill (progressive disclosure):
1) After deciding to use a skill, open its SKILL.md. Read only enough to follow the workflow.
2) When SKILL.md references relative paths (e.g., scripts/foo.py), resolve them relative to the skill directory listed above first, and only consider other paths if needed.
3) If SKILL.md points to extra folders such as references/, load only the specific files needed for the request; don't bulk-load everything.
4) If scripts/ exist, prefer running or patching them instead of retyping large code blocks.
5) If assets/ or templates exist, reuse them instead of recreating from scratch.
- Coordination and sequencing:
- If multiple skills apply, choose the minimal set that covers the request and state the order you'll use them.
- Announce which skill(s) you're using and why (one short line). If you skip an obvious skill, say why.
- Context hygiene:
- Keep context small: summarize long sections instead of pasting them; only load extra files when needed.
- Avoid deep reference-chasing: prefer opening only files directly linked from SKILL.md unless you're blocked.
- When variants exist (frameworks, providers, domains), pick only the relevant reference file(s) and note that choice.
- Safety and fallback: If a skill can't be applied cleanly (missing files, unclear instructions), state the issue, pick the next-best approach, and continue.

## Instruction Priority

Superpowers skills override default system prompt behavior, but **user instructions always take precedence**:

1. **User's explicit instructions** (CLAUDE.md, GEMINI.md, AGENTS.md, direct requests) 鈥?highest priority
2. **Superpowers skills** 鈥?override default system behavior where they conflict
3. **Default system prompt** 鈥?lowest priority

If CLAUDE.md, GEMINI.md, or AGENTS.md says "don't use TDD" and a skill says "always use TDD," follow the user's instructions. The user is in control.

## How to Access Skills

**In Claude Code:** Use the `Skill` tool. When you invoke a skill, its content is loaded and presented to you鈥攆ollow it directly. Never use the Read tool on skill files.

**In Gemini CLI:** Skills activate via the `activate_skill` tool. Gemini loads skill metadata at session start and activates the full content on demand.

**In other environments:** Check your platform's documentation for how skills are loaded.

## Platform Adaptation

Skills use Claude Code tool names. Non-CC platforms: see `references/codex-tools.md` (Codex) for tool equivalents. Gemini CLI users get the tool mapping loaded automatically via GEMINI.md.

# Using Skills

## The Rule

**Invoke relevant or requested skills BEFORE any response or action.** Even a 1% chance a skill might apply means that you should invoke the skill to check. If an invoked skill turns out to be wrong for the situation, you don't need to use it.

```dot
digraph skill_flow {
    "User message received" [shape=doublecircle];
    "About to EnterPlanMode?" [shape=doublecircle];
    "Already brainstormed?" [shape=diamond];
    "Invoke brainstorming skill" [shape=box];
    "Might any skill apply?" [shape=diamond];
    "Invoke Skill tool" [shape=box];
    "Announce: 'Using [skill] to [purpose]'" [shape=box];
    "Has checklist?" [shape=diamond];
    "Create TodoWrite todo per item" [shape=box];
    "Follow skill exactly" [shape=box];
    "Respond (including clarifications)" [shape=doublecircle];

    "About to EnterPlanMode?" -> "Already brainstormed?";
    "Already brainstormed?" -> "Invoke brainstorming skill" [label="no"];
    "Already brainstormed?" -> "Might any skill apply?" [label="yes"];
    "Invoke brainstorming skill" -> "Might any skill apply?";

    "User message received" -> "Might any skill apply?";
    "Might any skill apply?" -> "Invoke Skill tool" [label="yes, even 1%"];
    "Might any skill apply?" -> "Respond (including clarifications)" [label="definitely not"];
    "Invoke Skill tool" -> "Announce: 'Using [skill] to [purpose]'";
    "Announce: 'Using [skill] to [purpose]'" -> "Has checklist?";
    "Has checklist?" -> "Create TodoWrite todo per item" [label="yes"];
    "Has checklist?" -> "Follow skill exactly" [label="no"];
    "Create TodoWrite todo per item" -> "Follow skill exactly";
}
```

## Red Flags

These thoughts mean STOP鈥攜ou're rationalizing:

| Thought | Reality |
|---------|---------|
| "This is just a simple question" | Questions are tasks. Check for skills. |
| "I need more context first" | Skill check comes BEFORE clarifying questions. |
| "Let me explore the codebase first" | Skills tell you HOW to explore. Check first. |
| "I can check git/files quickly" | Files lack conversation context. Check for skills. |
| "Let me gather information first" | Skills tell you HOW to gather information. |
| "This doesn't need a formal skill" | If a skill exists, use it. |
| "I remember this skill" | Skills evolve. Read current version. |
| "This doesn't count as a task" | Action = task. Check for skills. |
| "The skill is overkill" | Simple things become complex. Use it. |
| "I'll just do this one thing first" | Check BEFORE doing anything. |
| "This feels productive" | Undisciplined action wastes time. Skills prevent this. |
| "I know what that means" | Knowing the concept 鈮?using the skill. Invoke it. |

## Skill Priority

When multiple skills could apply, use this order:

1. **Process skills first** (brainstorming, debugging) - these determine HOW to approach the task
2. **Implementation skills second** (frontend-design, mcp-builder) - these guide execution

"Let's build X" 鈫?brainstorming first, then implementation skills.
"Fix this bug" 鈫?debugging first, then domain-specific skills.

## Skill Types

**Rigid** (TDD, debugging): Follow exactly. Don't adapt away discipline.

**Flexible** (patterns): Adapt principles to context.

The skill itself tells you which.

## User Instructions

Instructions say WHAT, not HOW. "Add X" or "Fix Y" doesn't mean skip workflows.

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass, field
import logging
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Callable, Dict, List, Optional

from domain.video.config import VideoPipelineConfig
from domain.video.stages import (
    run_stage0_clean,
    run_stage1_transcode,
    run_stage2_silence,
    run_stage3_repair,
    run_stage4_asr,
    run_stage5_ai_text,
    run_stage6_5_resub,
    run_stage6_clip,
    run_stage7_correct,
    run_stage7_subtitle,
    run_stage8_cover,
    run_stage9_organize,
)
from domain.video.stages.base import StageResult
from domain.video.stages.utils import probe_duration_seconds


@dataclass
class PipelineResult:
    success: bool
    output_file: Optional[str] = None
    error_message: Optional[str] = None
    executed_stages: List[str] = field(default_factory=list)
    performance_summary: str = ""
    current_stage: int = 0
    last_stage: Optional[str] = None
    failed_stage: Optional[str] = None
    performance_report: Optional[Any] = None


class VideoPipeline:
    """Internal multi-stage video pipeline."""

    def __init__(
        self,
        config: VideoPipelineConfig,
        logger: Optional[logging.Logger] = None,
        performance_tracker: Any = None,
        resource_monitor: Any = None,
    ) -> None:
        self.config = config
        self.logger = logger or logging.getLogger("clonecut.domain.video.pipeline")
        self.performance_tracker = performance_tracker
        self.resource_monitor = resource_monitor
        self._stages: List[tuple[str, Callable[..., StageResult]]] = [
            ("stage0_clean", self._stage0),
            ("stage1_transcode", self._stage1),
            ("stage2_silence", self._stage2),
            ("stage3_repair", self._stage3),
            ("stage4_asr", self._stage4),
            ("stage5_ai_text", self._stage5),
            ("stage6_clip", self._stage6),
            ("stage6_5_resub", self._stage6_5),
            ("stage7_correct", self._stage7_correct),
            ("stage7_subtitle", self._stage7),
            ("stage8_cover", self._stage8),
            ("stage9_organize", self._stage9),
        ]

    def run(
        self,
        input_video: str,
        task_id: str,
        start_from_stage: int = 0,
        forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
    ) -> PipelineResult:
        current = input_video
        executed: List[str] = []
        stage_start = max(0, int(start_from_stage))
        context: Dict[str, Any] = {"forum_post_info": _normalize_forum_post_info(forum_post_info)}
        last_stage_index = max(0, min(stage_start, len(self._stages) - 1 if self._stages else 0))
        last_stage_name: Optional[str] = None
        gpu_stage_indexes = {1, 2, 4, 6}
        tracking_started = False

        if self.performance_tracker is not None:
            try:
                path = Path(input_video)
                file_size_mb = 0.0
                if path.exists():
                    file_size_mb = path.stat().st_size / (1024 * 1024)
                duration_seconds = probe_duration_seconds(input_video)
                self.performance_tracker.start_video_processing(
                    task_id=task_id,
                    video_filename=path.name,
                    original_filename=path.name,
                    file_size_mb=file_size_mb,
                    video_duration_seconds=duration_seconds,
                )
                tracking_started = True
            except Exception as exc:
                self.logger.warning("start performance tracking failed: task=%s err=%s", task_id, exc)

        for idx, (stage_name, handler) in enumerate(self._stages):
            if idx < stage_start:
                continue

            if self.resource_monitor is not None:
                try:
                    self.resource_monitor.record_step_resource(
                        step_num=idx,
                        step_name=stage_name,
                        task_id=task_id,
                    )
                except Exception as exc:
                    self.logger.debug("resource snapshot failed: task=%s stage=%s err=%s", task_id, stage_name, exc)
            if self.performance_tracker is not None:
                try:
                    self.performance_tracker.start_stage(
                        task_id=task_id,
                        stage_name=stage_name,
                        gpu_accelerated=(idx in gpu_stage_indexes),
                    )
                except Exception:
                    pass
            try:
                result = handler(current, task_id=task_id, stage_name=stage_name, context=context)
            except Exception as exc:
                if self.performance_tracker is not None:
                    try:
                        self.performance_tracker.end_stage(
                            task_id=task_id,
                            stage_name=stage_name,
                            success=False,
                            error_message=str(exc),
                        )
                        self.performance_tracker.add_error(task_id, str(exc))
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                perf_report = self._finish_tracking(task_id, tracking_started)
                return PipelineResult(
                    success=False,
                    output_file=current,
                    error_message=f"{stage_name} exception: {exc}",
                    executed_stages=executed,
                    current_stage=idx,
                    last_stage=last_stage_name,
                    failed_stage=stage_name,
                    performance_report=perf_report,
                )

            executed.append(stage_name)
            last_stage_index = idx
            last_stage_name = stage_name
            if not result.success:
                if self.performance_tracker is not None:
                    try:
                        self.performance_tracker.end_stage(
                            task_id=task_id,
                            stage_name=stage_name,
                            success=False,
                            error_message=str(result.error_message or ""),
                        )
                        self.performance_tracker.add_error(
                            task_id,
                            str(result.error_message or f"{stage_name} failed"),
                        )
                    except Exception:
                        pass
                perf_report = self._finish_tracking(task_id, tracking_started)
                return PipelineResult(
                    success=False,
                    output_file=current,
                    error_message=result.error_message or f"{stage_name} failed",
                    executed_stages=executed,
                    current_stage=idx,
                    last_stage=last_stage_name,
                    failed_stage=stage_name,
                    performance_report=perf_report,
                )
            if self.performance_tracker is not None:
                try:
                    self.performance_tracker.end_stage(
                        task_id=task_id,
                        stage_name=stage_name,
                        success=True,
                    )
                except Exception:
                    pass
            if result.output_file:
                current = result.output_file

        perf_report = self._finish_tracking(task_id, tracking_started)
        summary = f"internal pipeline executed stages={len(executed)}"
        if perf_report is not None:
            try:
                ratio = float(getattr(perf_report, "processing_speed_ratio", 0.0))
                if ratio > 0:
                    summary = f"internal pipeline executed stages={len(executed)} speed={ratio:.2f}x"
            except Exception:
                pass
        return PipelineResult(
            success=True,
            output_file=current,
            executed_stages=executed,
            performance_summary=summary,
            current_stage=last_stage_index,
            last_stage=last_stage_name,
            performance_report=perf_report,
        )

    def _finish_tracking(self, task_id: str, tracking_started: bool) -> Optional[Any]:
        if not tracking_started or self.performance_tracker is None:
            return None
        try:
            return self.performance_tracker.end_video_processing(task_id)
        except Exception:
            return None

    def _stage0(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage0_clean(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

    def _stage1(self, current: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, context: Dict[str, Any]) -> StageResult:
        self.logger.debug("pipeline stage start: %s task=%s", stage_name, task_id)
        return run_stage1_transcode(current, self.config.output_dir, task_id)

def _normalize_forum_post_info(raw: Optional[dict]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    if not isinstance(raw, dict):
        return {}

    info: Dict[str, Any] = dict(raw)
    hotwords = _normalize_hotwords(info.get("hotwords"))
    info["hotwords"] = hotwords

    speaker = _pick_first_text(
        info,
        keys=("speaker", "speaker_id", "spk", "target_speaker"),
    )
    if speaker:
        info["speaker"] = speaker

    cover_titles = _normalize_cover_titles(info.get("cover_titles"))
    cover_up = _pick_first_text(info, keys=("cover_title_up", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?))
    cover_middle = _pick_first_text(info, keys=("cover_title_middle", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?))
    cover_down = _pick_first_text(info, keys=("cover_title_down", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?))

    if not cover_up and len(cover_titles) >= 1:
        cover_up = cover_titles[0]
    if not cover_middle and len(cover_titles) >= 2:
        cover_middle = cover_titles[1]
    if not cover_down and len(cover_titles) >= 3:
        cover_down = cover_titles[2]

    compact_titles = [item for item in (cover_up, cover_middle, cover_down) if item]
    if compact_titles:
        cover_titles = compact_titles

    info["cover_title_up"] = cover_up
    info["cover_title_middle"] = cover_middle
    info["cover_title_down"] = cover_down
    info["灏侀潰鏍囬涓?] = cover_up
    info["灏侀潰鏍囬涓?] = cover_middle
    info["灏侀潰鏍囬涓?] = cover_down
    info["cover_titles"] = cover_titles

    return info


def _normalize_cover_titles(value: Any) -> List[str]:
    if not isinstance(value, list):
        return []
    output: List[str] = []
    seen: set[str] = set()
    for item in value:
        if isinstance(item, dict):
            text = str(item.get("text", "")).strip()
        else:
            text = str(item or "").strip()
        normalized = " ".join(text.split())
        if not normalized:
            continue
        if normalized in seen:
            continue
        seen.add(normalized)
        output.append(normalized)
        if len(output) >= 3:
            break
    return output


def _normalize_hotwords(value: Any) -> List[str]:
    candidates: List[str] = []
    if isinstance(value, list):
        candidates = [str(item).strip() for item in value]
    elif isinstance(value, str):
        candidates = [item.strip() for item in value.replace("\uFF0C", ",").split(",")]

    output: List[str] = []
    seen: set[str] = set()
    for item in candidates:
        text = str(item or "").strip()
        if not text:
            continue
        dedup_key = text.lower()
        if dedup_key in seen:
            continue
        seen.add(dedup_key)
        output.append(text)
    return output


def _pick_first_text(info: Dict[str, Any], keys: tuple[str, ...]) -> str:
    for key in keys:
        value = str(info.get(key, "")).strip()
        if value:
            return value
    return ""

def ensure_stage_dir(output_dir: str, task_id: str) -> Path:
    stage_dir = Path(output_dir) / task_id / "_stages"
    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    return stage_dir


def probe_duration_seconds(_input_video: str) -> float:
    # Keep this deterministic and dependency-free in the skeleton phase.
    return 0.0


def stage_artifact_path(output_dir: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, suffix: str) -> Path:
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    return stage_dir / f"{task_id}_{stage_name}{suffix}"

import json

from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir, stage_artifact_path


def _resolve_segments(**_kwargs: Any) -> tuple[list[dict], str, str, list[dict]]:
    # Compatibility shim for tests/consumers that monkeypatch this hook.
    return ([], "timeline_fallback", "skeleton resolver", [])


def run_stage4_asr(
    input_video: str,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
    hotwords: Optional[List[str]] = None,
    speaker: Optional[str] = None,
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage4 input missing")

    srt_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage4_asr_subtitles", ".srt")
    transcript_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage4_asr_transcript", ".txt")
    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage4_asr_manifest", ".json")

    engine = "stub_asr"
    sidecar_backend = os.getenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "").strip().lower()
    prefer_sidecar = os.getenv("CLONECUT_ASR_PREFER_SIDECAR", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    sidecar_hint = Path(f"{Path(input_video).with_suffix('')}.srt")
    sidecar_raw = os.getenv("CLONECUT_ASR_SIDECAR_PATH", "").strip()
    sidecar_path = Path(sidecar_raw).expanduser() if sidecar_raw else sidecar_hint
    attempts: list[dict] = []

    use_sidecar = (sidecar_backend == "sidecar") or (sidecar_backend == "auto" and prefer_sidecar)
    if use_sidecar and sidecar_path.exists() and sidecar_path.is_file():
        attempts.append({"backend": "sidecar", "ok": True})
        srt_path.write_text(sidecar_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"), encoding="utf-8")
        engine = "sidecar_srt"
    else:
        attempts.append({"backend": sidecar_backend or "stub", "ok": False})
        _, resolved_engine, _, _ = _resolve_segments(input_video=input_video, output_dir=output_dir, task_id=task_id)
        engine = str(resolved_engine or "timeline_fallback")
        srt_path.write_text(
            "1\n00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000\nclonecut stage4 stub\n",
            encoding="utf-8",
        )

    transcript_path.write_text("clonecut stage4 transcript stub\n", encoding="utf-8")
    info = forum_post_info or {}
    raw_hotwords = hotwords if hotwords is not None else info.get("hotwords", [])
    if not isinstance(raw_hotwords, list):
        raw_hotwords = []
    normalized_hotwords = [str(item).strip() for item in raw_hotwords if str(item).strip()]
    dedup_hotwords: list[str] = []
    seen: set[str] = set()
    for item in normalized_hotwords:
        if item.lower() in seen:
            continue
        seen.add(item.lower())
        dedup_hotwords.append(item)

    strict = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    fallback_used = engine in {"timeline_fallback", "stub_asr"}
    strict_rejected = strict and fallback_used
    result_success = not strict_rejected
    payload: Dict[str, Any] = {
        "engine": engine,
        "task_id": task_id,
        "input_video": str(source),
        "subtitle_file": str(srt_path),
        "transcript_file": str(transcript_path),
        "hotwords": dedup_hotwords,
        "hotword_count": len(dedup_hotwords),
        "speaker": str(speaker or info.get("speaker", "")).strip(),
        "forum_post_info": info,
        "attempts": attempts,
        "fallback_used": fallback_used,
        "strict_rejected": strict_rejected,
    }
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")

    return StageResult(
        success=result_success,
        output_file=str(source),
        error_message="strict equivalence rejected stage4 fallback" if strict_rejected else None,
        artifacts={
            "subtitle_file": str(srt_path),
            "transcript_file": str(transcript_path),
            "manifest_file": str(manifest_path),
        },
        metadata={"engine": engine},
    )


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage4_asr(*args, **kwargs)

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os

from typing import Any
from typing import Optional

from .base import StageResult

def run_stage5_ai_text(
    input_video: str,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    task_root = Path(output_dir) / task_id
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage5 input missing")

    script_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage5_ai_script", ".txt")
    pointer_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage5_script_path", ".txt")
    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage5_ai_manifest", ".json")
    clip_text_path = task_root / "clip_text.txt"
    script_text = "Script Draft\n\nKey Points:\n- skeleton output\n"
    script_path.write_text(script_text, encoding="utf-8")
    clip_text_path.write_text(script_text, encoding="utf-8")
    pointer_path.write_text(str(script_path), encoding="utf-8")
    use_forum_keywords = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_USE_FORUM_KEYWORDS", "true").strip().lower() == "true"
    hotwords = []
    raw_hotwords = forum_post_info.get("hotwords", []) if isinstance(forum_post_info, dict) else []
    if use_forum_keywords:
        seen: set[str] = set()
        for item in raw_hotwords:
            text = str(item).strip()
            if not text or text in seen:
                continue
            seen.add(text)
            hotwords.append(text)
    llm_use_factory = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_LLM_USE_FACTORY", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    llm_provider = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE5_LLM_PROVIDER", "rule").strip().lower()
    engine = "rule_based"
    llm_error = ""
    fallback_used = False
    strict_rejected = False
    if llm_use_factory and llm_provider == "rule":
        engine = "llm_factory:rule"
    elif llm_use_factory and llm_provider != "rule":
        engine = "rule_based"
        llm_error = "missing api_key for provider"
        fallback_used = True

    manifest_path.write_text(
        json.dumps(
            {
                "task_id": task_id,
                "forum_post_info": forum_post_info or {},
                "engine": engine,
                "keywords": hotwords,
                "use_forum_keywords": use_forum_keywords,
                "forum_keyword_count": len(hotwords),
                "llm_use_factory": llm_use_factory,
                "llm_error": llm_error,
                "fallback_used": fallback_used,
                "strict_rejected": strict_rejected,
            },
            ensure_ascii=False,
            indent=2,
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(source), artifacts={"manifest_file": str(manifest_path)})


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage5_ai_text(*args, **kwargs)

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
import shutil
import subprocess
from typing import Any

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir, probe_duration_seconds, stage_artifact_path


def ffmpeg_exists() -> bool:
    return shutil.which("ffmpeg") is not None


def run_ffmpeg(args: list[str], timeout_seconds: int = 1800) -> tuple[bool, str]:
    try:
        completed = subprocess.run(args, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=timeout_seconds, check=False)
        if completed.returncode == 0:
            return True, ""
        return False, completed.stderr or completed.stdout or f"exit={completed.returncode}"
    except Exception as exc:
        return False, str(exc)


def _build_clip_ranges(
    *,
    subtitle_path: Path,
    video_duration: float,
    max_duration: float = 0.0,
    target_speaker: str = "",
) -> tuple[list[tuple[float, float]], str]:
    if not subtitle_path.exists():
        return ([(0.0, max(0.1, float(video_duration or 1.0)))], "merged=1 missing_subtitle")
    text = subtitle_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    # Minimal deterministic shape: split by subtitle blocks and create simple 1s ranges.
    blocks = [item for item in text.split("\n\n") if item.strip()]
    ranges: list[tuple[float, float]] = []
    matched = 0
    total = 0
    cursor = 0.0
    for block in blocks:
        lines = [line.strip() for line in block.splitlines() if line.strip()]
        if len(lines) < 3:
            continue
        total += 1
        content = " ".join(lines[2:]).strip()
        if target_speaker and f"[{target_speaker}]" not in content:
            continue
        matched += 1
        ranges.append((cursor, min(cursor + 1.0, float(video_duration or 1.0))))
        cursor += 1.5
    if not ranges:
        ranges = [(0.0, min(1.0, float(video_duration or 1.0)))]
    if max_duration and max_duration > 0:
        limited: list[tuple[float, float]] = []
        spent = 0.0
        for start, end in ranges:
            dur = max(0.0, end - start)
            if spent + dur <= max_duration:
                limited.append((start, end))
                spent += dur
                continue
            remain = max_duration - spent
            if remain > 0:
                limited.append((start, start + remain))
            break
        ranges = limited or ranges[:1]
    detail = f"merged={len(ranges)}"
    if target_speaker:
        detail += f" speaker_filter target={target_speaker} matched={matched}/{max(total,1)}"
    return ranges, detail


def _render_trim_seconds(source: Path, target: Path, target_seconds: float) -> tuple[bool, str]:
    codec = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_VIDEO_CODEC", "").strip() or os.getenv("CLONECUT_VIDEO_CODEC", "").strip()
    codec = codec or "libx264"
    cmd = ["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-t", f"{target_seconds:.3f}", "-c:v", codec, str(target)]
    ok, err = run_ffmpeg(cmd)
    if ok:
        return True, ""
    if codec.endswith("_nvenc") and "nvenc" in err.lower():
        cmd = ["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-t", f"{target_seconds:.3f}", "-c:v", "libx264", str(target)]
        return run_ffmpeg(cmd)
    return False, err


def _resolve_clip_text_input(output_dir: str, task_id: str) -> tuple[str, str]:
    env_path = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_CLIP_TEXT_PATH", "").strip()
    candidate_paths: list[Path] = []
    if env_path:
        candidate_paths.append(Path(env_path))
    candidate_paths.append(Path(output_dir) / task_id / "clip_text.txt")

    for path in candidate_paths:
        if not path.exists() or not path.is_file():
            continue
        try:
            return path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"), str(path)
        except Exception:
            continue
    return "", ""


def run_stage6_clip(input_video: str, output_dir: str, task_id: str) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage6 input missing")

    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_clip_manifest", ".json")
    out_copy = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_clip_copy", ".mp4")
    strict = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    payload: dict[str, Any] = {"task_id": task_id, "method": "copy_fallback", "fallback_used": False, "detail": ""}

    guide_path = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_DURATION_GUIDE_PATH", "").strip()
    clip_text_match = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_CLIP_TEXT_MATCH", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    subtitle_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage4_asr_subtitles", ".srt")
    stage4_manifest = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage4_asr_manifest", ".json")
    target_speaker = ""
    if stage4_manifest.exists():
        try:
            target_speaker = str(json.loads(stage4_manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8")).get("speaker", "")).strip()
        except Exception:
            target_speaker = ""

    if ffmpeg_exists():
        out_clip = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_clip", ".mp4")
        if guide_path:
            seconds = probe_duration_seconds(guide_path)
            ok, err = _render_trim_seconds(source=source, target=out_clip, target_seconds=max(0.1, seconds))
            if ok:
                payload["method"] = "duration_guide_trim"
                manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
                return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(out_clip))
            payload["error"] = err
        elif clip_text_match:
            clip_text, clip_text_source = _resolve_clip_text_input(output_dir=output_dir, task_id=task_id)
            payload["clip_text_used"] = bool(clip_text.strip())
            payload["clip_text_source"] = clip_text_source
            ok, err = run_ffmpeg(["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-c", "copy", str(out_clip)])
            if ok:
                payload["method"] = "subtitle_clip_text_concat"
                manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
                return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(out_clip))
            payload["error"] = err
        else:
            ranges, detail = _build_clip_ranges(
                subtitle_path=subtitle_path,
                video_duration=max(1.0, probe_duration_seconds(input_video)),
                max_duration=0.0,
                target_speaker=target_speaker,
            )
            payload["detail"] = detail
            ok, err = run_ffmpeg(["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-c", "copy", str(out_clip)])
            if ok:
                payload["method"] = "subtitle_concat" if target_speaker else "subtitle_concat"
                payload["ranges"] = ranges
                manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
                return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(out_clip))
            payload["error"] = err

    payload["fallback_used"] = True
    if strict:
        payload["method"] = "strict_rejected"
        manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=str(source), error_message="strict equivalence rejected stage6 fallback")

    shutil.copyfile(source, out_copy)
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(out_copy))


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage6_clip(*args, **kwargs)

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir, stage_artifact_path


def _resolve_segments(**_kwargs: Any) -> tuple[list[dict], str, str, list[dict]]:
    return ([], "timeline_fallback", "skeleton resolver", [])


def run_stage6_5_resub(input_video: str, output_dir: str, task_id: str) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage6_5 input missing")

    srt_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_5_resub_subtitles", ".srt")
    ass_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_5_resub_subtitles", ".ass")
    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_5_resub_manifest", ".json")

    mode = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_5_MODE", "auto").strip().lower()
    strict = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    method = "legacy_normalize" if mode == "legacy" else "re_asr"
    engine = "sidecar_srt" if os.getenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "").strip().lower() == "sidecar" else "stub_asr"
    fallback_used = False
    if mode == "auto":
        _, method, _, _ = _resolve_segments(input_video=input_video, output_dir=output_dir, task_id=task_id)
        fallback_used = method == "timeline_fallback"
        if method == "timeline_fallback":
            engine = "timeline_fallback"

    strict_rejected = strict and method == "timeline_fallback"
    text = "1\n00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000\nhello world\n"
    srt_path.write_text(text, encoding="utf-8")
    ass_path.write_text("[Script Info]\nTitle: stage6_5 stub\n", encoding="utf-8")
    manifest_path.write_text(
        json.dumps(
            {
                "task_id": task_id,
                "method": method,
                "engine": engine,
                "fallback_used": fallback_used,
                "strict_rejected": strict_rejected,
            },
            ensure_ascii=False,
            indent=2,
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    return StageResult(
        success=not strict_rejected,
        output_file=str(source),
        error_message="strict equivalence rejected stage6_5 fallback" if strict_rejected else None,
    )


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage6_5_resub(*args, **kwargs)

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any
import re

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir, stage_artifact_path


def _normalize_text(text: str) -> str:
    cleaned = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", text).strip()
    cleaned = cleaned.replace(" ,", ",")
    return cleaned


def run_stage7_correct(input_video: str, output_dir: str, task_id: str) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage7_correct input missing")

    source_srt = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_5_resub_subtitles", ".srt")
    corrected_srt = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage7_correct_subtitles", ".srt")
    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage7_correct_manifest", ".json")

    if not source_srt.exists():
        source_srt.write_text("1\n00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000\nstage7 correct stub\n", encoding="utf-8")

    enabled = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE7_CORRECT_ENABLE", "true").strip().lower() == "true"
    mode = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE7_CORRECT_MODE", "rule").strip().lower()
    strict = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE", "false").strip().lower() == "true"

    source_text = source_srt.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    out_text = source_text
    method = "disabled_copy"
    engine = "disabled"
    changed_count = 0

    if enabled:
        if mode == "llm":
            api_key = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY", "").strip()
            model = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE7_CORRECT_LLM_MODEL", "").strip()
            if not api_key or not model:
                method = "strict_rejected" if strict else "copy_fallback"
                engine = "llm_failed"
                manifest_path.write_text(
                    json.dumps(
                        {
                            "task_id": task_id,
                            "method": method,
                            "engine": engine,
                            "changed_line_count": 0,
                        },
                        ensure_ascii=False,
                        indent=2,
                    ),
                    encoding="utf-8",
                )
                if strict:
                    return StageResult(
                        success=False,
                        output_file=str(source),
                        error_message="strict equivalence rejected stage7 correct llm fallback",
                    )
            else:
                method = "corrected"
                engine = "llm_stub"
        if mode == "rule":
            method = "corrected"
            engine = "rule_based"
            replacements = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE7_CORRECT_REPLACEMENTS", "").strip()
            transformed = source_text
            if replacements:
                for pair in replacements.split("|"):
                    if "=>" not in pair:
                        continue
                    old, new = pair.split("=>", 1)
                    transformed = transformed.replace(old.strip(), new.strip())
            normalized_lines = [_normalize_text(line) if "-->" not in line and not line.isdigit() else line for line in transformed.splitlines()]
            out_text = "\n".join(normalized_lines).strip() + "\n"
            changed_count = 0 if out_text == source_text else 1

    if not corrected_srt.exists() or method != "strict_rejected":
        corrected_srt.write_text(out_text, encoding="utf-8")

    manifest_path.write_text(
        json.dumps(
            {
                "task_id": task_id,
                "method": method,
                "engine": engine,
                "changed_line_count": changed_count,
            },
            ensure_ascii=False,
            indent=2,
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(source))


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage7_correct(*args, **kwargs)

def run_ffmpeg(args: list[str], timeout_seconds: int = 1800) -> tuple[bool, str]:
    try:
        completed = subprocess.run(args, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=timeout_seconds, check=False)
        if completed.returncode == 0:
            return True, ""
        return False, completed.stderr or completed.stdout or f"exit={completed.returncode}"

def _probe_video_resolution(_source: Path) -> tuple[int, int]:
    return (1280, 720)


def run_stage7_subtitle(input_video: str, output_dir: str, task_id: str) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage7_subtitle input missing")

    stage_dir = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage7_subtitle_manifest", ".json").parent
    subtitle_ass = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_5_resub_subtitles", ".ass")
    subtitle_srt = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage7_correct_subtitles", ".srt")
    if not subtitle_srt.exists():
        subtitle_srt = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_5_resub_subtitles", ".srt")

    output = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage7_subtitle", ".mp4")
    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage7_subtitle_manifest", ".json")
    mode = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STAGE7_MODE", "auto").strip().lower()
    strict = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE", "false").strip().lower() == "true"

    method = "copy_fallback"
    fallback_used = False
    if ffmpeg_exists() and (mode in {"auto", "burn"}):
        vf_expr = ""
        if subtitle_ass.exists():
            vf_expr = f"ass={subtitle_ass}"
        else:
            _, h = _probe_video_resolution(source)
            font_size = max(24, int(round(h * 0.05)))
            vf_expr = f"subtitles={subtitle_srt}:force_style='Fontsize={font_size}'"
        ok, err = run_ffmpeg(["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-vf", vf_expr, str(output)])
        if ok and output.exists():
            method = "burn_subtitle"
            manifest_path.write_text(
                json.dumps({"task_id": task_id, "method": method, "vf_expr": vf_expr}, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
                encoding="utf-8",
            )
            return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(output))
        fallback_used = True
    else:
        fallback_used = True

    if strict and fallback_used:
        manifest_path.write_text(
            json.dumps(
                {"task_id": task_id, "method": "strict_rejected", "fallback_used": True},
                ensure_ascii=False,
                indent=2,
            ),
            encoding="utf-8",
        )
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=str(source), error_message="strict equivalence rejected stage7 fallback")

    shutil.copyfile(source, output)
    manifest_path.write_text(
        json.dumps({"task_id": task_id, "method": method, "fallback_used": fallback_used}, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(output))


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage7_subtitle(*args, **kwargs)

def _render_title_overlay_image(output_path: str, width: int, height: int, lines: list[str]) -> tuple[bool, str]:
    # Deterministic placeholder image artifact for compatibility-only phase.
    payload = f"overlay {width}x{height} {' | '.join(lines)}".encode("utf-8")
    Path(output_path).write_bytes(payload)
    return True, ""


def run_stage8_cover(
    input_video: str,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    *,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage8 input missing")

    info = forum_post_info or {}
    raw_cover_titles = info.get("cover_titles") if isinstance(info.get("cover_titles"), list) else []
    cover_titles: list[str] = []
    for item in raw_cover_titles:
        if isinstance(item, dict):
            text = str(item.get("text", "")).strip()
        else:
            text = str(item or "").strip()
        if text:
            cover_titles.append(text)
    if not cover_titles:
        for key in ("cover_title_up", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?, "cover_title_middle", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?, "cover_title_down", "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?):
            text = str(info.get(key, "")).strip()
            if text:
                cover_titles.append(text)

    title_txt = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover_title", ".txt")
    title_txt.write_text("\n".join(cover_titles) + ("\n" if cover_titles else ""), encoding="utf-8")
    output_video = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover", ".mp4")
    overlay_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover_overlay", ".png")
    subtitle_for_timing = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage7_correct_subtitles", ".srt")
    if not subtitle_for_timing.exists():
        subtitle_for_timing = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage6_5_resub_subtitles", ".srt")

    method = "title_text_only"
    overlay_duration_seconds = 0.0
    fallback_used = False
    strict = os.getenv("CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE", "false").strip().lower() == "true"
    if ffmpeg_exists():
        _render_title_overlay_image(str(overlay_path), 1280, 720, cover_titles)
        overlay_duration_seconds = 1.7 if subtitle_for_timing.exists() else 2.0
        filter_expr = f"[0:v][1:v]overlay=0:0:enable='between(t,0,{overlay_duration_seconds:.3f})'"
        ok, err = run_ffmpeg(
            ["ffmpeg", "-y", "-i", str(source), "-i", str(overlay_path), "-filter_complex", filter_expr, str(output_video)]
        )
        if ok and output_video.exists():
            method = "video_title_overlay"
        else:
            fallback_used = True
            shutil.copyfile(source, output_video)
    else:
        fallback_used = True
        if strict:
            method = "strict_rejected"
        else:
            shutil.copyfile(source, output_video)

    strict_rejected = strict and fallback_used
    payload = {
        "task_id": task_id,
        "cover_titles": cover_titles,
        "cover_title_lines": cover_titles,
        "cover_title_up": str(info.get("cover_title_up", "")),
        "cover_title_middle": str(info.get("cover_title_middle", "")),
        "cover_title_down": str(info.get("cover_title_down", "")),
        "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?: str(info.get("灏侀潰鏍囬涓?, "")),
        "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?: str(info.get("灏侀潰鏍囬涓?, "")),
        "灏侀潰鏍囬涓?: str(info.get("灏侀潰鏍囬涓?, "")),
        "method": method,
        "fallback_used": fallback_used,
        "strict_rejected": strict_rejected,
        "overlay_duration_seconds": overlay_duration_seconds,
    }
    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage8_cover_manifest", ".json")
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    return StageResult(
        success=not strict_rejected,
        output_file=str(output_video if output_video.exists() else source),
        error_message="strict equivalence rejected stage8 fallback" if strict_rejected else None,
        artifacts={"manifest_file": str(manifest_path), "title_file": str(title_txt)},
    )


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage8_cover(*args, **kwargs)

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import shutil
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Optional
from typing import Any

from .base import StageResult
from .utils import ensure_stage_dir, stage_artifact_path


def run_stage9_organize(
    input_video: str,
    *,
    output_dir: str,
    task_id: str,
    keep_intermediate_files: bool,
    forum_post_info: Optional[dict] = None,
    original_filename: str = "",
) -> StageResult:
    source = Path(input_video)
    stage_dir = ensure_stage_dir(output_dir, task_id)
    if not source.exists():
        return StageResult(success=False, output_file=input_video, error_message="stage9 input missing")

    info = forum_post_info or {}
    candidate_name = str(original_filename or info.get("original_filename", "")).strip()
    preferred_stem = Path(candidate_name).stem.strip() if candidate_name else ""
    final_dir_name = preferred_stem or task_id

    task_root = Path(output_dir) / final_dir_name
    task_root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    final_output = task_root / f"{final_dir_name}_final.mp4"
    legacy_output = task_root / f"{task_id}.mp4"

    if source.resolve() != final_output.resolve():
        shutil.copyfile(source, final_output)
    if source.resolve() != legacy_output.resolve():
        shutil.copyfile(source, legacy_output)

    archive_dir = task_root / f"{task_id}_artifacts"
    logs_dir = task_root / "logs"
    archive_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    logs_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    if keep_intermediate_files:
        if stage_dir.exists():
            archive_stages = archive_dir / "_stages"
            logs_stages = logs_dir / "_stages"
            if archive_stages.exists():
                shutil.rmtree(archive_stages)
            if logs_stages.exists():
                shutil.rmtree(logs_stages)
            shutil.copytree(stage_dir, archive_stages, dirs_exist_ok=True)
            shutil.copytree(stage_dir, logs_stages, dirs_exist_ok=True)

    manifest_path = stage_artifact_path(output_dir, task_id, "stage9_organize_manifest", ".json")
    payload = {
        "task_id": task_id,
        "final_output": str(final_output),
        "legacy_output": str(legacy_output),
        "keep_intermediate_files": bool(keep_intermediate_files),
        "original_filename": str(original_filename or ""),
        "forum_post_info": forum_post_info or {},
        "archive_dir": str(archive_dir),
        "final_output_dir": str(task_root),
    }
    manifest_path.write_text(json.dumps(payload, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2), encoding="utf-8")
    return StageResult(success=True, output_file=str(final_output), artifacts={"manifest_file": str(manifest_path)})


def run(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> StageResult:
    return run_stage9_organize(*args, **kwargs)

def test_stage4_prefers_sidecar_subtitle(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "sidecar")
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    sidecar = tmp_path / "input.srt"
    sidecar.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,500",
                "hello world",
                "",
                "2",
                "00:00:01,500 --> 00:00:03,000",
                "second line",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    result = stage4_asr.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v1")
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file
    assert Path(str(result.output_file)).exists()

    srt = out_dir / "v1" / "_stages" / "v1_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    transcript = out_dir / "v1" / "_stages" / "v1_stage4_asr_transcript.txt"
    manifest = out_dir / "v1" / "_stages" / "v1_stage4_asr_manifest.json"
    assert srt.exists()
    assert transcript.exists()
    assert manifest.exists()
    assert "hello world" in srt.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("engine") == "sidecar_srt"
    assert payload.get("fallback_used") is False
    attempts = payload.get("attempts") or []
    assert attempts and attempts[0].get("backend") == "sidecar"

def test_build_clip_ranges_respects_max_duration(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_PAD_BEFORE_SECONDS", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_PAD_AFTER_SECONDS", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_MERGE_GAP_SECONDS", raising=False)

        subtitle_path=subtitle,
        video_duration=12.0,
        max_duration=3,
    )
    assert ranges

    assert total <= 3.01
    assert "merged=" in detail


def test_stage6_trim_prefers_stage6_codec_env(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]

    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_VIDEO_CODEC", "libx264")

    captured: list[list[str]] = []

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured.append(list(args))
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)

    assert ok is True
    assert error == ""

def test_stage6_trim_gpu_codec_failure_downgrades_to_libx264(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    target = tmp_path / "out.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"input-video")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE6_VIDEO_CODEC", "h264_nvenc")

    captured: list[list[str]] = []
    calls = {"count": 0}

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured.append(list(args))
        calls["count"] += 1
        if calls["count"] == 1:
            return False, "No NVENC capable devices found"
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)
    ok, error = stage6_clip._render_trim_seconds(source=source, target=target, target_seconds=3.0)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]

    assert ok is True
    assert error == ""
    codecs = [cmd[cmd.index("-c:v") + 1] for cmd in captured]
    assert codecs == ["h264_nvenc", "libx264"]

    )

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        out = Path(args[-1])
        out.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        out.write_bytes(b"trimmed-video")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage6_clip, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)

    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    result = stage6_clip.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id="v6_guide")
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file
    output_path = Path(str(result.output_file))
    assert output_path.exists()
    assert output_path.read_bytes() == b"trimmed-video"

    manifest_path = out_dir / "v6_guide" / "_stages" / "v6_guide_stage6_clip_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("method") == "duration_guide_trim"

import json
from pathlib import Path

from domain.video.stages import stage7_correct, stage7_subtitle


def _write_basic_srt(path: Path, text: str) -> None:
    path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    path.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000",
                text,
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage2_silence, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: False)

    captured = {"cmd": []}

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]

def test_stage2_silenceremove_gpu_codec_failure_downgrades_to_libx264(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    target = tmp_path / "out.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE2_VIDEO_CODEC", "h264_nvenc")

    captured: list[list[str]] = []
    calls = {"count": 0}

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured.append(list(args))
        calls["count"] += 1
        if calls["count"] == 1:
            return False, "No NVENC capable devices found"
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage2_silence, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)
    ok, error = stage2_silence._run_ffmpeg_silence_remove(source=source, target=target)  # type: ignore[attr-defined]

    assert ok is True
    assert error == ""
    assert len(captured) == 2
    codecs = [cmd[cmd.index("-c:v") + 1] for cmd in captured]
    assert codecs == ["h264_nvenc", "libx264"]

    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")

    task_id = "v7_ass"

    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    srt = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage6_5_resub_subtitles.srt"
    ass = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage6_5_resub_subtitles.ass"
    srt.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:01,000",
                "hello srt",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    ass.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "[Script Info]",
                "Title: ass subtitle",
                "",
                "[Events]",
                "Format: Layer, Start, End, Style, Name, MarginL, MarginR, MarginV, Effect, Text",
                "Dialogue: 0,0:00:00.00,0:00:01.00,Default,,0,0,0,,hello ass",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STAGE7_MODE", "burn")
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage7_subtitle, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: True)
    captured = {"cmd": []}

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured["cmd"] = list(args)
        Path(args[-1]).write_bytes(b"burned-video")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage7_subtitle, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)
    result = stage7_subtitle.run(input_video=str(source), output_dir=str(out_dir), task_id=task_id)
    assert result.success
    vf_expr = captured["cmd"][captured["cmd"].index("-vf") + 1]
    assert vf_expr.startswith("ass=")

def test_stage9_archives_stage_artifacts(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    task_id = "v9"

    (stage_dir / "note.txt").write_text("stage artifact", encoding="utf-8")

    source = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage8_cover.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"final-video")

    result = stage9_organize.run(
        input_video=str(source),
        output_dir=str(out_dir),
        task_id=task_id,
        keep_intermediate_files=True,
    )
    assert result.success
    assert result.output_file

    final_path = out_dir / task_id / f"{task_id}_final.mp4"
    assert final_path.exists()
    legacy_final_path = out_dir / task_id / f"{task_id}.mp4"
    assert legacy_final_path.exists()

    archive_dir = out_dir / task_id / f"{task_id}_artifacts"
    assert archive_dir.exists()
    assert (archive_dir / "_stages" / "note.txt").exists()
    assert (out_dir / task_id / "logs" / "_stages" / "note.txt").exists()

    manifest = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage9_organize_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("archive_dir")
    assert payload.get("final_output_dir") == str(out_dir / task_id)

def test_stage8_applies_video_title_overlay_with_subtitle_timing(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    task_id = "v8_overlay"
    stage_dir = out_dir / task_id / "_stages"
    stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    subtitle = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage7_correct_subtitles.srt"
    subtitle.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:02,000 --> 00:00:04,000",
                "first subtitle",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage8_cover, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: True)
    captured = {"cmds": []}

    def fake_render_overlay(output_path, width, height, lines):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        Path(output_path).parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        Path(output_path).write_bytes(b"overlay-image")
        return True, ""

    def fake_run_ffmpeg(args, timeout_seconds=1800):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured["cmds"].append(list(args))
        Path(args[-1]).parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        Path(args[-1]).write_bytes(b"generated")
        return True, ""

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage8_cover, "_render_title_overlay_image", fake_render_overlay)
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage8_cover, "run_ffmpeg", fake_run_ffmpeg)

    result = stage8_cover.run(
        input_video=str(source),
        output_dir=str(out_dir),
        task_id=task_id,
        forum_post_info={"cover_titles": ["up-line", "down-line"]},
    )
    assert result.success

    manifest = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage8_cover_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert "video_title_overlay" in str(payload.get("method", ""))
    assert payload.get("overlay_duration_seconds") == 1.7

    overlay_cmd = captured["cmds"][-1]
    filter_expr = overlay_cmd[overlay_cmd.index("-filter_complex") + 1]
    assert "between(t,0,1.700)" in filter_expr


def test_stage8_strict_mode_rejects_when_overlay_not_applied(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    out_dir = tmp_path / "out"
    task_id = "v8_strict"
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_STRICT_EQUIVALENCE", "true")
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage8_cover, "ffmpeg_exists", lambda: False)

    result = stage8_cover.run(
        input_video=str(source),
        output_dir=str(out_dir),
        task_id=task_id,
        forum_post_info={"cover_title_up": "strict-title"},
    )
    assert result.success is False
    assert "strict equivalence" in str(result.error_message)

    stage_dir = out_dir / task_id / "_stages"
    manifest = stage_dir / f"{task_id}_stage8_cover_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("strict_rejected") is True
    assert payload.get("fallback_used") is True

def test_internal_pipeline_skeleton_runs(tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"

    assert "stage7_subtitle" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage8_cover" in result.executed_stages
    assert "stage9_organize" in result.executed_stages
    assert result.current_stage == 11
    assert result.failed_stage is None
    srt = tmp_path / "out" / "video-1" / "_stages" / "video-1_stage4_asr_subtitles.srt"
    manifest = tmp_path / "out" / "video-1" / "_stages" / "video-1_stage8_cover_manifest.json"

    assert not result.success

def test_pipeline_stage4_manifest_contains_forum_context(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_BACKEND", "sidecar")
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    sidecar = tmp_path / "shared.srt"
    sidecar.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "1",
                "00:00:00,000 --> 00:00:02,000",
                "pipeline context subtitle",
                "",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    monkeypatch.setenv("CLONECUT_ASR_SIDECAR_PATH", str(sidecar))

    cfg = VideoPipelineConfig(output_dir=str(tmp_path / "out"))
    pipeline = VideoPipeline(cfg)
    result = pipeline.run(
        input_video=str(source),
        task_id="video-ctx",
        forum_post_info={"hotwords": ["topic-a", "topic-b"], "speaker": "spk-1"},
    )

    assert result.success
    manifest = tmp_path / "out" / "video-ctx" / "_stages" / "video-ctx_stage4_asr_manifest.json"
    payload = json.loads(manifest.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    assert payload.get("engine") == "sidecar_srt"
    assert payload.get("hotwords") == ["topic-a", "topic-b"]
    assert payload.get("hotword_count") == 2
    assert payload.get("speaker") == "spk-1"


def test_pipeline_stage4_receives_explicit_hotwords(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"fake-video")
    cfg = VideoPipelineConfig(output_dir=str(tmp_path / "out"))
    pipeline = VideoPipeline(cfg)
    captured: dict = {}

    def fake_stage4(input_video, output_dir, task_id, *, forum_post_info=None, hotwords=None, speaker=None):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured["forum_post_info"] = forum_post_info
        captured["hotwords"] = hotwords
        captured["speaker"] = speaker
        return StageResult(success=True, output_file=input_video)

    monkeypatch.setattr("domain.video.pipeline.run_stage4_asr", fake_stage4)
    result = pipeline._stage4(  # type: ignore[attr-defined]
        str(source),
        task_id="video-stage4-ctx",
        stage_name="stage4_asr",
        context={
            "forum_post_info": {
                "hotwords": ["topic-a", "topic-b", "topic-a"],
                "speaker": "spk-x",
            }
        },
    )

    assert result.success
    assert captured["hotwords"] == ["topic-a", "topic-b"]
    assert captured["speaker"] == "spk-x"

from __future__ import annotations

from pathlib import Path
from types import SimpleNamespace

from apps.gradio_ui.backend import GradioBackend, GradioBackendConfig


def test_gradio_backend_run_asr_clip_subtitle_manual_chain(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    source = tmp_path / "demo.mp4"
    source.write_bytes(b"video")

    backend = GradioBackend(GradioBackendConfig(output_dir=str(tmp_path / "out")))

    calls = {"asr": 0, "clip": 0, "sub": 0}

    def fake_stage4(input_video, output_dir, task_id, forum_post_info=None, hotwords=None, speaker=None):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        calls["asr"] += 1
        assert Path(input_video).exists()
        assert output_dir == str(tmp_path / "out")
        assert isinstance(hotwords, list)
        return SimpleNamespace(success=True, output_file=str(source), error_message=None)

    def fake_stage6(input_video, output_dir, task_id):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        calls["clip"] += 1
        return SimpleNamespace(success=True, output_file=str(source), error_message=None)

    def fake_stage65(input_video, output_dir, task_id):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        calls["sub"] += 1
        return SimpleNamespace(success=True, output_file=str(source), error_message=None)

    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.gradio_ui.backend.run_stage4_asr", fake_stage4)
    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.gradio_ui.backend.run_stage6_clip", fake_stage6)
    monkeypatch.setattr("apps.gradio_ui.backend.run_stage6_5_resub", fake_stage65)

    asr = backend.run_asr(str(source), hotwords="热词A,热词B", speaker="spk1")
    assert asr["success"] is True

    clip = backend.run_clip(str(source), clip_text="第一句\n第二句", speaker="spk1")
    assert clip["success"] is True

    subtitle = backend.run_subtitle(str(source), subtitle_format="ass")
    assert subtitle["success"] is True

    chain = backend.run_manual_chain(
        str(source),
        hotwords="热词A,热词B",
        clip_text="第一句",
        speaker="spk1",
        subtitle_format="ass",
    )
    assert chain["success"] is True
    assert calls["asr"] >= 2
    assert calls["clip"] >= 2
    assert calls["sub"] >= 2


def test_gradio_backend_handles_missing_input_file(tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    backend = GradioBackend(GradioBackendConfig(output_dir=str(tmp_path / "out")))

    result = backend.run_asr(str(tmp_path / "missing.mp4"))
    assert result["success"] is False
    assert "not found" in str(result.get("error", ""))

class RetryableUploadError(RuntimeError):
    """Upload failure that should be retried by queue scheduler."""


class NonRetryableUploadError(RuntimeError):
    """Upload failure that must not be retried by queue scheduler."""

    def start(self) -> None:
        if any(thread.is_alive() for thread in self.worker_threads):
            return

        if self.internal_pipeline_runner is not None:
            self.internal_pipeline_runner.start()
        self.resource_monitor.start()
        recovered = self._recover_stuck_tasks()
        restored_retries = self._restore_retry_schedule()
        self.stop_event.clear()
        self.worker_threads = []
        self._spawn_workers("download", self.max_download_workers, self._download_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("process", self.max_process_workers, self._process_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("upload", self.max_upload_workers, self._upload_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("retry", 1, self._retry_scheduler_loop)
        self._spawn_workers("zombie", 1, self._zombie_cleaner_loop)

        self.logger.info(
            "worker adapters: tts_enabled=%s tts_engine=%s tts_http_ready=%s video_cmd_enabled=%s internal_pipeline=%s redis_registry=%s redis_queue=%s recovered=%s restored_retries=%s",
            self.tts_adapter_enabled,
            self.tts_engine_mode,
            self.tts_http_adapter.is_ready(),
            self.video_adapter.is_enabled(),
            self.internal_pipeline_enabled,
            self.registry.is_persistent(),
            self.use_redis_queue,
            recovered,
            restored_retries,
        )
        self.logger.info(
            "worker pools started: download=%s process=%s upload=%s retry_scheduler=%s zombie_timeout=%ss zombie_by_status=%s internal_runner=%s warm_pool=%s",
            self.max_download_workers,
            self.max_process_workers,
            self.max_upload_workers,
            1,
            self.zombie_timeout_seconds,
            self.zombie_timeout_by_status_seconds,
            self.internal_pipeline_runner_mode,
            self.internal_pipeline_pool_size if self.internal_pipeline_runner is not None else 0,
        )

    def stop(self) -> None:
        self.stop_event.set()
        for thread in self.worker_threads:
            thread.join(timeout=2.0)
        if self.internal_pipeline_runner is not None:
            self.internal_pipeline_runner.stop()
        self.resource_monitor.stop()
        self.logger.info("worker service stopped")

    def submit(self, raw_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Tuple[bool, str, Optional[str]]:
        try:
            task = self._build_task(raw_data)
        except ValueError as exc:
            return False, "", str(exc)

        existing_task_id = self.queue_adapter.check_duplicate(task)
        if existing_task_id:
            self.logger.info(
                "duplicate task ignored: incoming=%s existing=%s",
                task.task_id,
                existing_task_id,
            )
            return True, existing_task_id, None

        self._persist_task(task)
        self.queue_adapter.remember_dedup(task, ttl_seconds=self.dedup_ttl_seconds)
        self._enqueue_task(self._initial_queue_for_task(task), task)

        with self.lock:
            self.stats["received"] += 1

        self.logger.info(
            "task received: task_id=%s type=%s queued=%s",
            task.task_id,
            task.task_type.value,
            self._initial_queue_for_task(task),
        )
        return True, task.task_id, None

    def get_status(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        queue_sizes = self.queue_adapter.get_queue_sizes()
        queued_total = (
            int(queue_sizes.get("download", 0))
            + int(queue_sizes.get("process", 0))
            + int(queue_sizes.get("upload", 0))
        )
        task_status_counts = self.get_task_status_counts()

        with self.lock:
            running = sum(self.active_workers.values())
            stats = dict(self.stats)
            active_workers = dict(self.active_workers)
        active_task_count = (
            int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.PENDING.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.ASSIGNED.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value, 0))
            + int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value, 0))
        )
        status_metrics = {
            "total": int(task_status_counts.get("total", 0)),
            "completed": int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.COMPLETED.value, 0)),
            "failed": int(task_status_counts.get(TaskStatus.FAILED.value, 0)),
            "active": int(active_task_count),
            "zombie": int(stats["zombie_reclaimed"]),
            "retried": int(stats["retried"]),
            "received": int(stats["received"]),
        }

        return {
            "status": "online",
            "is_busy": running > 0 or queued_total > 0,
            "total_queue_size": queued_total + running,
            "queue_sizes": queue_sizes,
            "queues": {
                "download": int(queue_sizes.get("download", 0)),
                "process": int(queue_sizes.get("process", 0)),
                "upload": int(queue_sizes.get("upload", 0)),
                "pending": queued_total,
                "processing": active_workers.get("process", 0),
                "completed": stats["completed"],
                "failed": stats["failed"],
                "retried": stats["retried"],
                "received": stats["received"],
                "active": active_task_count,
                "total": int(task_status_counts.get("total", 0)),
                "zombie_reclaimed": stats["zombie_reclaimed"],
                "zombie": stats["zombie_reclaimed"],
            },
            "workers": active_workers,
            "status_metrics": status_metrics,
            "task_status_counts": task_status_counts,
            "uptime_seconds": int(max(0, time.time() - self.booted_at)),
            "timestamp": time.time(),
        }

    def get_resources(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        return self.resource_monitor.get_current()

    def get_resources_history(self, minutes: int = 60) -> list:
        return self.resource_monitor.get_history(minutes=minutes)

    def get_task(self, task_id: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        task = self.registry.get(task_id)
        if task is None:
            return None
        return task.to_dict()

    def get_task_status_counts(self) -> Dict[str, int]:
        counts: Dict[str, int] = {}
        for status in self._queryable_statuses():
            counts[status.value] = int(self.registry.count_by_status(status))
        counts["total"] = sum(counts.values())
        return counts

    def list_tasks(
        self,
        status: Optional[str] = None,
        limit: int = 20,
        offset: int = 0,
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        size = max(1, min(200, int(limit)))
        start = max(0, int(offset))
        target_statuses = self._resolve_status_filter(status)
        read_limit = min(5000, start + size)

        if len(target_statuses) == 1:
            selected = target_statuses[0]
            total = int(self.registry.count_by_status(selected))
            tasks = self.registry.list_by_status(selected, limit=max(1, read_limit))
        else:
            total = 0
            merged: Dict[str, UnifiedTask] = {}
            for st in target_statuses:
                total += int(self.registry.count_by_status(st))
                for task in self.registry.list_by_status(st, limit=max(1, read_limit)):
                    merged[task.task_id] = task
            tasks = list(merged.values())
            tasks.sort(key=lambda item: item.created_at, reverse=True)

        selected_tasks = tasks[start : start + size]
        return {
            "total": total,
            "limit": size,
            "offset": start,
            "tasks": [item.to_dict() for item in selected_tasks],
        }

        task = self.registry.get(task_id)
        if task is None:
            return False, "task not found"
        if task.status == TaskStatus.CANCELLED:
            return True, ""
