        if speaker:
            merged["speaker"] = speaker

        original_filename = self._resolve_original_filename(
            forum_post_info=merged,
            payload=payload,
            metadata=metadata,
            source_url="",
        )
        if original_filename:
            merged["original_filename"] = original_filename
        return merged

    def _normalize_text_list(self, *values: Any) -> List[str]:
        output: List[str] = []
        seen: set[str] = set()
        for value in values:
            items: List[str] = []
            if isinstance(value, list):
                items = [str(item or "").strip() for item in value]
            elif isinstance(value, str):
                items = [item.strip() for item in value.replace("\uFF0C", ",").split(",")]
            for item in items:
                normalized = " ".join(item.split())
                if not normalized:
                    continue
                dedup_key = normalized.lower()
                if dedup_key in seen:
                    continue
                seen.add(dedup_key)
                output.append(normalized)
        return output

    def _pick_first_text(self, *values: Any) -> str:
        for value in values:
            text = str(value or "").strip()
            if text:
                return text
        return ""

    def _sanitize_filename(self, value: str) -> str:
        text = str(value or "").strip()
        if not text:
            return ""
        text = text.replace("\\", "/").split("/")[-1].strip()
        text = re.sub(r"[\x00-\x1f]", "", text)
        text = re.sub(r"[<>:\"/\\\\|?*]+", "_", text)
        text = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", text).strip().strip(".")
        return text

    def _init_task_storage(self) -> Optional[SqliteStorageAdapter]:
        db_path = os.getenv("CLONECUT_DB_PATH", "data/clonecut.db")
        try:
            return SqliteStorageAdapter(db_path=db_path, logger=self.logger)
        except Exception as exc:
            self.logger.warning("sqlite storage disabled: %s", exc)
            return None

    def _save_task_snapshot(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        self._sync_task_metadata(task)
        if self.task_storage is None:
            return
        self.task_storage.save_task(task)

    def _persist_task(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        self._sync_task_metadata(task)
        self.registry.add(task)
        self._save_task_snapshot(task)

    def _sync_task_metadata(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        metadata["current_stage"] = int(task.current_stage)
        metadata["max_retries"] = int(task.max_retries)
        metadata["retry_count"] = int(task.retry_count)
        if task.stage_checkpoint:
            metadata["stage_checkpoint"] = task.stage_checkpoint
        else:
            metadata.pop("stage_checkpoint", None)
        task.metadata = metadata

    def _transition_status(self, task: UnifiedTask, status: TaskStatus, strict: bool = True) -> bool:
        result = self.registry.update_status(task.task_id, status)
        if result.ok:
            task.status = status
            if status in {TaskStatus.PENDING, TaskStatus.FAILED, TaskStatus.CANCELLED}:
                task.started_at = None
            return True
        if strict:
            raise RuntimeError(result.reason or f"status transition failed: {task.task_id}")
        return False

    def _mark_task_active(self, task_id: str, active: bool) -> None:
        with self.lock:
            if active:
                self.active_task_ids.add(task_id)
            else:
                self.active_task_ids.discard(task_id)

    def _schedule_retry(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> bool:
        if task.status != TaskStatus.FAILED:
            return False
        retryable = bool((task.metadata or {}).get("retryable_failure", True))
        if not retryable:
            return False
        max_retries = max(0, int(task.max_retries))
        if task.retry_count >= max_retries:
            return False

        delay = self._retry_delay_seconds(task, task.retry_count)
        retry_count = task.retry_count + 1
        due_at = time.time() + delay
        task.retry_count = retry_count
        task.metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        task.metadata["retry_due_at"] = due_at
        task.metadata["retry_delay_seconds"] = delay
        self._persist_task(task)

        with self.lock:
            self.retry_index[task.task_id] = (due_at, task)
            heapq.heappush(self.retry_heap, (due_at, task.task_id))
            self.stats["retried"] += 1
        return True

    def _retry_delay_seconds(self, task: UnifiedTask, retry_count_before_increment: int) -> int:
        failed_from = str((task.metadata or {}).get("failed_from_status", "")).strip().lower()
        backoff = self.retry_backoff_seconds or [5]
        if failed_from == TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value:
            backoff = self.upload_retry_backoff_seconds or [1, 2, 4]
        idx = min(max(0, int(retry_count_before_increment)), len(backoff) - 1)
        return int(backoff[idx])

    def _is_retryable_failure(self, error: Exception, failed_from: TaskStatus) -> bool:
        if failed_from != TaskStatus.UPLOADING:
            return True
        if isinstance(error, RetryableUploadError):
            return True
        if isinstance(error, NonRetryableUploadError):
            return False
        return False

    def _remove_retry_schedule(self, task_id: str) -> None:
        with self.lock:
            self.retry_index.pop(task_id, None)

    def _retry_scheduler_loop(self) -> None:
        while not self.stop_event.is_set():
            ready = self._dequeue_ready_retries()
            for task in ready:
                self._enqueue_retry_task(task)
            self.stop_event.wait(self.retry_check_interval_seconds)

    def _dequeue_ready_retries(self) -> List[UnifiedTask]:
        now_ts = time.time()
        ready: List[UnifiedTask] = []
        with self.lock:
            while self.retry_heap:
                due_at, task_id = self.retry_heap[0]
                if due_at > now_ts:
                    break
                heapq.heappop(self.retry_heap)
                indexed = self.retry_index.get(task_id)
                if indexed is None:
                    continue
                idx_due_at, task = indexed
                if idx_due_at != due_at:
                    continue
                self.retry_index.pop(task_id, None)
                ready.append(task)
        return ready

    def _enqueue_retry_task(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> None:
        queue_name = self._queue_for_retry_task(task)
        task.metadata = dict(task.metadata or {})
        task.metadata.pop("retry_due_at", None)
        task.metadata.pop("retry_delay_seconds", None)
        task.metadata.pop("retryable_failure", None)
        task.error_message = None
        task.completed_at = None
        task.started_at = None
        transitioned = self._transition_status(task, TaskStatus.PENDING, strict=False)
        if not transitioned:
            task.status = TaskStatus.PENDING
            self._persist_task(task)
        else:
            self._persist_task(task)
        if queue_name == "upload":
            transitioned_upload = self._transition_status(task, TaskStatus.PROCESSING, strict=False)
            if not transitioned_upload:
                task.status = TaskStatus.PROCESSING
            self._persist_task(task)
        self._enqueue_task(queue_name, task)
        self.logger.info(
            "task retry enqueued: task_id=%s retry_count=%s/%s queue=%s",
            task.task_id,
            task.retry_count,
            task.max_retries,
            queue_name,
        )

    def _queue_for_retry_task(self, task: UnifiedTask) -> str:
        failed_from = str((task.metadata or {}).get("failed_from_status", "")).strip().lower()
        if failed_from == TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value and self._has_uploadable_output(task):
            return "upload"
        if failed_from == TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING.value and self._needs_download(task):
            return "download"
        if failed_from == TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value:
            return "process"
        return self._initial_queue_for_task(task)

    def _restore_retry_schedule(self) -> int:
        if not self.registry.is_persistent():
            return 0
        tasks = self.registry.list_by_status(TaskStatus.FAILED, limit=5000)
        restored = 0
        now_ts = time.time()
        for task in tasks:
            if int(task.retry_count) >= int(task.max_retries):
                continue
            retry_due_at_raw = (task.metadata or {}).get("retry_due_at")
            try:
                retry_due_at = float(retry_due_at_raw)
            except Exception:
                retry_due_at = now_ts
            with self.lock:
                self.retry_index[task.task_id] = (retry_due_at, task)
                heapq.heappush(self.retry_heap, (retry_due_at, task.task_id))
            restored += 1
        return restored

    def _zombie_cleaner_loop(self) -> None:
        while not self.stop_event.is_set():
            reclaimed = self._reclaim_zombies_once()
            if reclaimed > 0:
                with self.lock:
                    self.stats["zombie_reclaimed"] += reclaimed
            self.stop_event.wait(self.zombie_check_interval_seconds)

    def _reclaim_zombies_once(self) -> int:
        running_statuses = [
            TaskStatus.PENDING,
            TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING,
            TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
            TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
        ]
        reclaimed = 0
        for status in running_statuses:
            tasks = self.registry.list_by_status(status, limit=2000)
            for task in tasks:
                if status != TaskStatus.PENDING:
                    with self.lock:
                        if task.task_id in self.active_task_ids:
                            continue
                if not self._is_zombie_task(task, status):
                    continue
                age = int((datetime.now() - (task.started_at or task.created_at)).total_seconds())
                error = RuntimeError(
                    f"zombie task reclaimed after {age}s in status={status.value}"
                )
                self._fail_task(task, error, failed_from=status)
                reclaimed += 1
        return reclaimed

    def _is_zombie_task(self, task: UnifiedTask, status: TaskStatus) -> bool:
        timeout_seconds = float(
            self.zombie_timeout_by_status_seconds.get(status.value, self.zombie_timeout_seconds)
        )
        if timeout_seconds <= 0:
            return False
        if status == TaskStatus.PENDING:
            started_at = task.created_at
        else:
            started_at = task.started_at or task.assigned_at or task.created_at
        if started_at is None:
            return False
        age = (datetime.now() - started_at).total_seconds()
        return age > timeout_seconds

    def _build_zombie_timeout_by_status(self) -> Dict[str, float]:
        mapping_raw = self._get_worker_cfg("zombie_timeout_by_status_seconds", {})
        mapping = mapping_raw if isinstance(mapping_raw, dict) else {}
        defaults = {
            TaskStatus.PENDING.value: float(self.zombie_timeout_seconds),
            TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING.value: float(self.zombie_timeout_seconds),
            TaskStatus.PROCESSING.value: float(self.zombie_timeout_seconds),
            TaskStatus.UPLOADING.value: float(self.zombie_timeout_seconds),
        }
        resolved: Dict[str, float] = {}
        for status_value, default in defaults.items():
            per_status_key = f"zombie_timeout_{status_value}_seconds"
            per_status_value = self._get_worker_cfg(per_status_key, None)
            if per_status_value is not None:
                resolved[status_value] = self._coerce_timeout_seconds(per_status_value, default)
                continue
            map_value = mapping.get(status_value)
            if map_value is not None:
                resolved[status_value] = self._coerce_timeout_seconds(map_value, default)
                continue
            resolved[status_value] = float(default)
        return resolved

    def _coerce_timeout_seconds(self, value: Any, default: float) -> float:
        try:
            return max(5.0, float(value))
        except Exception:
            return max(5.0, float(default))

    def _recover_stuck_tasks(self) -> int:
        if not self.registry.is_persistent():
            return 0

        recoverable = [
            TaskStatus.ASSIGNED,
            TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING,
            TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
            TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
        ]
        recovered = 0
        for status in recoverable:
            tasks = self.registry.list_by_status(status, limit=2000)
            for task in tasks:
                queue_name = self._recovery_queue_for_task(task, status)
                next_status = TaskStatus.PROCESSING if queue_name == "upload" else TaskStatus.PENDING
                task.status = next_status
                if next_status == TaskStatus.PENDING:
                    task.started_at = None
                else:
                    task.started_at = task.started_at or datetime.now()
                task.completed_at = None
                self._persist_task(task)
                self._enqueue_task(queue_name, task)
                recovered += 1
        return recovered

    def _recovery_queue_for_task(self, task: UnifiedTask, old_status: TaskStatus) -> str:
        if old_status == TaskStatus.UPLOADING and self._has_uploadable_output(task):
            return "upload"
        if old_status == TaskStatus.PROCESSING:
            return "process"
        if old_status == TaskStatus.FAILED:
            return self._queue_for_retry_task(task)
        if old_status == TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING and self._needs_download(task):
            return "download"
        return self._initial_queue_for_task(task)

    def _get_queue_cfg(self, key: str, default: Any) -> Any:
        raw_queue = {}
        if isinstance(getattr(self.config, "raw", None), dict):
            raw_queue = self.config.raw.get("queue", {}) or {}
        env_key = f"CLONECUT_QUEUE_{key}".upper()
        env_val = os.getenv(env_key)
        if env_val is not None:
            return self._cast_cfg_value(env_val, default)
        if key in raw_queue:
            return self._cast_cfg_value(raw_queue.get(key), default)
        return default

    def _parse_retry_backoff(self, raw: Any) -> List[int]:
        if isinstance(raw, list):
            values = raw
        elif isinstance(raw, str):
            text = raw.strip()
            values = [item.strip() for item in text.split(",") if item.strip()]
        else:
            values = [5, 10, 20]

        parsed: List[int] = []
        for item in values:
            try:
                parsed.append(max(1, int(item)))
            except Exception:
                continue
        if not parsed:
            parsed = [5, 10, 20]
        return parsed

    def _get_worker_cfg(self, key: str, default: Any) -> Any:
        raw_worker = {}
        if isinstance(getattr(self.config, "raw", None), dict):
            raw_worker = self.config.raw.get("worker", {}) or {}

        env_key = f"CLONECUT_WORKER_{key}".upper()
        env_val = os.getenv(env_key)
        if env_val is not None:
            return self._cast_cfg_value(env_val, default)
        if key in raw_worker:
            return self._cast_cfg_value(raw_worker.get(key), default)
        return default

    def _cast_cfg_value(self, value: Any, default: Any) -> Any:
        if isinstance(default, bool):
            if isinstance(value, bool):
                return value
            return str(value).strip().lower() == "true"
        if isinstance(default, int):
            try:
                return int(value)
            except Exception:
                return default
        if isinstance(default, float):
            try:
                return float(value)
            except Exception:
                return default
        return value

    def _bool_cfg(self, raw: Optional[str], default: bool) -> bool:
        if raw is None:
            return default
        return raw.strip().lower() == "true"

    def _extract_optional_bool(self, *values: Any) -> Optional[bool]:
        for value in values:
            if value is None:
                continue
            if isinstance(value, bool):
                return value
            text = str(value).strip().lower()
            if not text:
                continue
            if text in {"1", "true", "yes", "y", "on"}:
                return True
            if text in {"0", "false", "no", "n", "off"}:
                return False
        return None

    def _queryable_statuses(self) -> List[TaskStatus]:
        return [
            TaskStatus.PENDING,
            TaskStatus.ASSIGNED,
            TaskStatus.DOWNLOADING,
            TaskStatus.PROCESSING,
            TaskStatus.UPLOADING,
            TaskStatus.COMPLETED,
            TaskStatus.FAILED,
            TaskStatus.CANCELLED,
        ]

    def _resolve_status_filter(self, status: Optional[str]) -> List[TaskStatus]:
        if status is None:
            return self._queryable_statuses()
        raw = str(status).strip().lower()
        if not raw or raw == "all":
            return self._queryable_statuses()
        known = {item.value for item in self._queryable_statuses()}
        if raw not in known:
            raise ValueError(f"invalid status filter: {status}")
        return [parse_task_status(raw)]

def _build_funasr_model(config):
    """Create FunASR model without depending on removed lightweight modules."""
    if not MODELS_AVAILABLE:
        return None
    try:
        model_name = config.get(
            "funasr_model_asr",
            "iic/speech_seaco_paraformer_large_asr_nat-zh-cn-16k-common-vocab8404-pytorch",
        )
        vad_model = config.get("funasr_model_vad", "damo/speech_fsmn_vad_zh-cn-16k-common-pytorch")
        punc_model = config.get(
            "funasr_model_punc",
            "damo/punc_ct-transformer_zh-cn-common-vocab272727-pytorch",
        )
        spk_model = config.get("funasr_model_spk", "damo/speech_campplus_sv_zh-cn_16k-common")
        kwargs = {
            "model": model_name,
            "vad_model": vad_model,
            "punc_model": punc_model,
        }
        if spk_model:
            kwargs["spk_model"] = spk_model
        return AutoModel(**kwargs)
    except Exception:
        return None


def _apply_runtime_defaults(config):
    """Apply runtime-dependent defaults that should stay consistent across entrypoints."""
    has_gpu = check_gpu_available()
    if has_gpu:
        logging.info("妫€娴嬪埌NVIDIA GPU锛屽凡鍚敤GPU鍔犻€?)
        config["use_gpu"] = True
    else:
        logging.info("鏈娴嬪埌NVIDIA GPU锛屼娇鐢–PU妯″紡")
        config["use_gpu"] = False
        if config["silence_codec_v"] == "h264_nvenc":
            config["silence_codec_v"] = "h264"

    ensure_output_dir(config["output_dir"])

    if "enable_step1" not in config:
        config["enable_step1"] = True
    if "enable_step8" not in config:
        config["enable_step8"] = True
    if "enable_step9" not in config:
        config["enable_step9"] = True


def _load_audio_clipper(config):
    """Load the shared ASR clipper once per process."""
    audio_clipper = None
    if MODELS_AVAILABLE:
        console.print("\n[info]姝ｅ湪鍒濆鍖栬闊宠瘑鍒ā鍨?..[/info]")
        try:
            funasr_model = _build_funasr_model(config)

            if funasr_model is not None:
                audio_clipper = VideoClipper(funasr_model)
                audio_clipper.lang = 'zh'  # default to Chinese
                console.print("[green]鉁?璇煶璇嗗埆妯″瀷鍔犺浇鎴愬姛[/green]")
            else:
                console.print("[red]鉂?璇煶璇嗗埆妯″瀷鍔犺浇澶辫触[/red]")
                audio_clipper = None
        except Exception as e:
            console.print(f"[red]鉂?璇煶璇嗗埆妯″瀷鍔犺浇澶辫触: {e}[/red]")
            audio_clipper = None
    else:
        console.print("[warning]鏃犳硶瀵煎叆FunASR鎴朏unClip妯″潡锛岃闊宠瘑鍒拰鍓緫鍔熻兘灏嗕笉鍙敤銆俒/warning]")
    return audio_clipper


def _get_shared_audio_clipper(config):
    global _SHARED_AUDIO_CLIPPER
    if _SHARED_AUDIO_CLIPPER is not None:
        return _SHARED_AUDIO_CLIPPER

    with _SHARED_AUDIO_CLIPPER_LOCK:
        if _SHARED_AUDIO_CLIPPER is None:
            _SHARED_AUDIO_CLIPPER = _load_audio_clipper(config)
    return _SHARED_AUDIO_CLIPPER


def warm_pipeline_runtime(output_dir: Optional[str] = None) -> bool:
    """Preload heavy pipeline state so a long-lived worker process can stay warm."""
    load_env()
    config = get_config()
    if output_dir:
        config["output_dir"] = output_dir
    _apply_runtime_defaults(config)
    return _get_shared_audio_clipper(config) is not None


def init_pipeline():
    """
    鍒濆鍖栨祦姘寸嚎鐜
    
    Returns:
        tuple: (config, logger, timer, audio_clipper) 閰嶇疆銆佹棩蹇楄褰曞櫒銆佽鏃跺櫒鍜屾ā鍨嬪鐞嗗櫒
    """
    # 鍔犺浇鐜鍙橀噺
    load_env()
    
    # 鑾峰彇閰嶇疆鍙傛暟
    config = get_config()
    _apply_runtime_defaults(config)
    
    # 璁剧疆鏃ュ織璁板綍鍣?
    logger = setup_logger(config["output_dir"])
    logger.info("寮€濮嬭棰戝鐞嗘祦姘寸嚎")
    
    # 鍒濆鍖栬鏃跺櫒
    timer = StepTimer()

    audio_clipper = _get_shared_audio_clipper(config)
    
    return config, logger, timer, audio_clipper


def run_step(step_number, step_name, step_func, current_video, config, timer, audio_clipper, enabled=True):
    """
    杩愯鍗曚釜娴佹按绾挎楠?
    
    Args:
        step_number: 姝ラ缂栧彿
        step_name: 姝ラ鍚嶇О
        step_func: 姝ラ鍑芥暟
        current_video: 褰撳墠澶勭悊鐨勮棰戣矾寰?
        config: 閰嶇疆瀛楀吀
        timer: 璁℃椂鍣?
        audio_clipper: 棰勫姞杞界殑妯″瀷澶勭悊鍣?
        enabled: 姝ラ鏄惁鍚敤
        
    Returns:
        tuple: (success, output_file, duration_str) 鏄惁鎴愬姛銆佽緭鍑烘枃浠惰矾寰勩€佺敤鏃?
    """
    if not enabled:
        console.print(f"[warning]璺宠繃姝ラ{step_number}: {step_name} (宸茬鐢?[/warning]")
        logging.getLogger("FunClip").info(f"璺宠繃姝ラ{step_number}: {step_name} (宸茬鐢?")
        return True, current_video, None
    
    # 鏄剧ず姝ラ鏍囬
    print_step_header(step_number, step_name)
    
    # 濡傛灉褰撳墠瑙嗛涓嶄负绌猴紝鏄剧ず杈撳叆鏂囦欢淇℃伅
    if current_video:
        print_file_info("杈撳叆鏂囦欢", current_video)
    
    # 寮€濮嬭鏃跺苟璁板綍鏃ュ織
    timer.start_step()
    log_step_start(step_number, step_name, current_video)
    
    # 杩愯姝ラ
    success = False
    output_file = current_video
    try:
        # Special handling for steps that need the clipper
        if step_number in [4, 6, 6.5]:
            if audio_clipper is None:
                console.print(f"\n[error]姝ラ{step_number} ({step_name}) 闇€瑕佺殑妯″瀷鏈垚鍔熷姞杞斤紝宸茶烦杩囥€俒/error]")
                success = False
                output_file = current_video
            else:
                if step_number == 4 or step_number == 6.5: # 璇煶璇嗗埆
                    success, _ = step_func(current_video, config, audio_clipper)
                    output_file = current_video
                elif step_number == 6: # 瑙嗛鍓緫
                    success, output_file = step_func(current_video, config, audio_clipper)
        # 绗?姝ヤ笉鏀瑰彉瑙嗛鏂囦欢锛屼絾杩斿洖鐨勬槸鏂囨湰鏂囦欢璺緞
        elif step_number == 5:
            success, output_file = step_func(current_video, config)
        # 鍏朵粬姝ラ
        else:
            success, output_file = step_func(current_video, config)
    except Exception as e:
        logger = logging.getLogger("FunClip")
        logger.error(f"姝ラ{step_number}寮傚父: {str(e)}")
        console.print(f"\n[error]姝ラ{step_number}寮傚父: {str(e)}[/error]")
        success = False
    
    # 缁撴潫璁℃椂
    duration_str = timer.end_step(step_number, step_name)
    
    # 璁板綍鏃ュ織
    log_step_end(step_number, step_name, success, duration_str, output_file)
    
    # 鎵撳嵃缁撴灉
    print_step_result(step_number, success, duration_str, 
                     output_file if step_number not in [4, 5] else None)
    
    if success:
        # 澧炲姞鍋ュ．鎬ф鏌ワ細纭繚杈撳嚭鏄枃浠惰€屼笉鏄洰褰?
        if output_file and os.path.isdir(output_file):
            logger.error(f"姝ラ{step_number} ({step_name}) 杩斿洖浜嗕竴涓洰褰曡矾寰?'{output_file}' 鑰屼笉鏄枃浠惰矾寰勩€?)
            console.print(f"[error]閿欒锛氭楠step_number} ({step_name}) 澶勭悊澶辫触锛岃繑鍥炰簡鏃犳晥鐨勮緭鍑鸿矾寰勩€俒/error]")
            return False, current_video, duration_str # 杩斿洖澶辫触

        # 淇濆瓨鐘舵€?
        if step_number == 4:
            # 璇煶璇嗗埆涓嶇敓鎴愭柊瑙嗛锛屼娇鐢ㄧ浉鍚岃緭鍏ヨ緭鍑?
            save_state(step_number, current_video, current_video, config["output_dir"], step_name)
        else:
            save_state(step_number, current_video, output_file, config["output_dir"], step_name)
        
        # 涓诲姩璋冪敤鍨冨溇鏀堕泦鍣ㄩ噴鏀惧唴瀛?
        gc.collect()
        logger = logging.getLogger("FunClip")
        logger.info(f"姝ラ{step_number}鍐呭瓨宸查噴鏀?)
        
        # 鏄剧ず绯荤粺璧勬簮浣跨敤鎯呭喌
        # 璁板綍褰撳墠姝ラ鐨勮祫婧愪娇鐢ㄦ儏鍐?
        usage_str = monitor.record_step_resource(step_number, f"姝ラ{step_number}: {step_name}")
        print_resource_usage()
        
    return success, output_file, duration_str


def should_run_step(step_number, choice, is_pipeline=False):
    """
    鍒ゆ柇鏄惁搴旇杩愯鎸囧畾姝ラ
    
    Args:
        step_number: 姝ラ缂栧彿
        choice: 鐢ㄦ埛閫夋嫨
        is_pipeline: 鏄惁鏄祦姘寸嚎妯″紡
        
    Returns:
        bool: 鏄惁搴旇杩愯璇ユ楠?
    """
    return str(step_number) == choice or (choice == "10" and is_pipeline)


def _parse_optional_bool_arg(value):
    if value is None:
        return None
    if isinstance(value, bool):
        return value
    text = str(value).strip().lower()
    if not text:
        return None
    if text in {"1", "true", "yes", "y", "on"}:
        return True
    if text in {"0", "false", "no", "n", "off"}:
        return False
    return None


def _apply_non_interactive_overrides(config, args):
    config["non_interactive"] = True
    config["input_wait_time"] = 0

    if args.model:
        config["stage5_model_name"] = args.model
        config["model_name"] = args.model
    if args.file_encoding:
        config["stage5_file_encoding"] = args.file_encoding
    if args.enable_preprocess:
        config["stage5_use_preprocessor"] = True
    elif args.disable_preprocess:
        config["stage5_use_preprocessor"] = False
    if args.clip_text:
        config["stage6_clip_text"] = args.clip_text
    if args.clip_text_file:
        config["stage6_clip_text_file"] = args.clip_text_file

    organize_delete_original = _parse_optional_bool_arg(args.organize_delete_original)
    if organize_delete_original is not None:
        config["organize_delete_original"] = organize_delete_original


def _copy_forum_post_info(forum_post_info_json, output_dir, logger):
    if not forum_post_info_json:
        return None

    source = os.path.abspath(forum_post_info_json)
    if not os.path.exists(source):
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"forum_post_info.json not found: {source}")

    with open(source, "r", encoding="utf-8") as fh:
        payload = json.load(fh)

    target = os.path.join(output_dir, "forum_post_info.json")
    with open(target, "w", encoding="utf-8") as fh:
        json.dump(payload, fh, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)

    logger.info(f"璁哄潧涓婁笅鏂囧凡鍐欏叆: {target}")
    return target


def _build_parser():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description='瑙嗛澶勭悊娴佹按绾?)
    parser.add_argument('--input', help='杈撳叆瑙嗛鏂囦欢璺緞')
    parser.add_argument('--output', help='杈撳嚭鐩綍璺緞')
    parser.add_argument('--model', help='stage5 妯″瀷瑕嗙洊锛屼緥濡?qwen/openai/deepseek/kimi/g4f')
    parser.add_argument('--file-encoding', help='stage5 鏂囦欢缂栫爜瑕嗙洊锛屼緥濡?utf-8/gbk')
    parser.add_argument('--enable-preprocess', action='store_true', help='寮哄埗鍚敤 stage5 鏂囨湰棰勫鐞?)
    parser.add_argument('--disable-preprocess', action='store_true', help='寮哄埗绂佺敤 stage5 鏂囨湰棰勫鐞?)
    parser.add_argument('--clip-text', help='stage6 鍓緫鏂囨湰瑕嗙洊')
    parser.add_argument('--clip-text-file', help='stage6 鍓緫鏂囨湰鏂囦欢瑕嗙洊')
    parser.add_argument('--forum-post-info-json', help='澶嶅埗鍒拌緭鍑虹洰褰曚腑鐨?forum_post_info.json 璺緞')
    parser.add_argument('--organize-delete-original', help='鎺у埗 stage9 鏄惁鍒犻櫎鏍圭洰褰曞師濮嬫枃浠讹紝true/false')
    return parser


def run_pipeline_request(
    *,
    input_path: Optional[str] = None,
    output_dir: Optional[str] = None,
    model: Optional[str] = None,
    file_encoding: Optional[str] = None,
    enable_preprocess: bool = False,
    disable_preprocess: bool = False,
    clip_text: Optional[str] = None,
    clip_text_file: Optional[str] = None,
    forum_post_info_json: Optional[str] = None,
    organize_delete_original: Optional[str] = None,
) -> bool:
    args = SimpleNamespace(
        input=input_path,
        output=output_dir,
        model=model,
        file_encoding=file_encoding,
        enable_preprocess=enable_preprocess,
        disable_preprocess=disable_preprocess,
        clip_text=clip_text,
        clip_text_file=clip_text_file,
        forum_post_info_json=forum_post_info_json,
        organize_delete_original=organize_delete_original,
    )
    return _run_pipeline_with_args(args)


def _run_pipeline_with_args(args: Any):
    """
    杩愯瀹屾暣娴佹按绾?

    Returns:
        bool: 娴佹按绾挎槸鍚︽垚鍔熷畬鎴?
    """

    # 濡傛灉鏈夊懡浠よ鍙傛暟锛屽垯浣跨敤闈炰氦浜掓ā寮?
    non_interactive_mode = args.input is not None

    show_banner()

    try:
        # 鍒濆鍖?
        config, logger, timer, audio_clipper = init_pipeline()

        # 濡傛灉鎸囧畾浜嗚緭鍑虹洰褰曪紝鏇存柊閰嶇疆
        if args.output:
            config["output_dir"] = args.output
            ensure_output_dir(config["output_dir"])
            logger = setup_logger(config["output_dir"])
            logger.info("寮€濮嬭棰戝鐞嗘祦姘寸嚎")

        if non_interactive_mode:
            _apply_non_interactive_overrides(config, args)
            if args.forum_post_info_json:
                _copy_forum_post_info(args.forum_post_info_json, config["output_dir"], logger)
        
        # 闈炰氦浜掓ā寮忥細鐩存帴杩愯瀹屾暣娴佹按绾?
        if non_interactive_mode:
            choice = "10"  # 瀹屾暣娴佹按绾?
            is_pipeline = True
        else:
            # 鏄剧ず鑿滃崟骞惰幏鍙栫敤鎴烽€夋嫨
            show_menu()
            choice = get_user_choice()

            # 鍒ゆ柇鏄惁涓哄畬鏁存祦姘寸嚎妯″紡
            is_pipeline = (choice == "10")

        # 濡傛灉鏄墽琛屽叏閮ㄦ楠?10)锛屽厛鎵ц娓呯悊JSON鏂囦欢
        if is_pipeline and config["enable_step0"]:
            success, _, _ = run_step(
                0, "娓呯悊杈撳嚭鐩綍JSON鏂囦欢", step0_clean_json, None, config, timer, audio_clipper,
                enabled=True
            )
            if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
                console.print("[error]娓呯悊JSON鏂囦欢澶辫触锛屾牴鎹厤缃粓姝㈡祦姘寸嚎[/error]")
                logger.error("娓呯悊JSON鏂囦欢澶辫触锛屾牴鎹厤缃粓姝㈡祦姘寸嚎")
                return False
                
            # 娓呯悊瀹屾垚鍚庤緭鍑烘彁绀?
            console.print("\n[info]JSON鏂囦欢娓呯悊瀹屾垚锛岃杈撳叆闇€瑕佸鐞嗙殑瑙嗛鏂囦欢璺緞[/info]")
        
        # 濡傛灉鍗曠嫭鎵ц娓呯悊JSON鎿嶄綔
        elif choice == "0":
            success, _, _ = run_step(
                0, "娓呯悊杈撳嚭鐩綍JSON鏂囦欢", step0_clean_json, None, config, timer, audio_clipper,
                enabled=True
            )
            if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
                console.print("[error]娓呯悊JSON鏂囦欢澶辫触锛屾牴鎹厤缃粓姝㈡祦姘寸嚎[/error]")
                logger.error("娓呯悊JSON鏂囦欢澶辫触锛屾牴鎹厤缃粓姝㈡祦姘寸嚎")
                return False
                
            console.print("\n[success]娓呯悊JSON鏂囦欢瀹屾垚锛屾祦姘寸嚎缁撴潫[/success]")
            return True
        
        # 鑾峰彇涓婃鐘舵€?
        last_state = None
        if choice != "10":  # 鎵ц鍏ㄩ儴姝ラ鏃朵笉浣跨敤涓婃鐘舵€?
            last_state = load_state(config["output_dir"])
        
        # 鏍规嵁鐢ㄦ埛閫夋嫨鑾峰彇杈撳叆瑙嗛
        if non_interactive_mode:
            # 闈炰氦浜掓ā寮忥細浣跨敤鍛戒护琛屽弬鏁颁腑鐨勮緭鍏ユ枃浠?
            input_video = args.input
            if not input_video:
                console.print("[error]闈炰氦浜掓ā寮忎笅蹇呴』鎸囧畾 --input 鍙傛暟[/error]")
                return False
            if not os.path.exists(input_video):
                console.print(f"[error]閿欒: 鎵句笉鍒拌棰戞枃浠?{input_video}[/error]")
                return False
        elif choice == "10":
            # 鍏ㄩ儴姝ラ锛氬己鍒惰姹傜敤鎴疯緭鍏ユ柊瑙嗛璺緞锛屼笉浣跨敤鍘嗗彶璁板綍
            console.print("\n[info]璇疯緭鍏ヨ澶勭悊鐨勮棰戞枃浠惰矾寰?[/info]")
            input_video = input("> ").strip()
            if not input_video:
                console.print("[error]鏈緭鍏ヨ棰戣矾寰勶紝绋嬪簭閫€鍑篬/error]")
                return False
            if not os.path.exists(input_video):
                console.print(f"[error]閿欒: 鎵句笉鍒拌棰戞枃浠?{input_video}[/error]")
                return False
        elif choice != "0":  # 涓嶆槸娓呯悊JSON鐨勫崟鐙搷浣?
            input_video = get_input_video(config["output_dir"], int(choice) if choice.isdigit() else None, last_state)
            if not input_video:
                logger.error("鏈兘鑾峰彇鏈夋晥鐨勮緭鍏ヨ棰戯紝娴佹按绾跨粓姝?)
                return False
        else:
            # 娓呯悊JSON鎿嶄綔涓嶉渶瑕佽緭鍏ヨ棰?
            input_video = None
        
        # 淇濆瓨鍘熷杈撳叆瑙嗛璺緞锛堢敤浜庡悗缁枃浠舵暣鐞嗭級
        original_input_video = input_video if input_video else ""
        
        # 褰撳墠澶勭悊鐨勮棰戣矾寰?
        current_video = input_video if input_video else ""
        
        # 姝ラ0: 娓呯悊JSON鏂囦欢 - 濡傛灉涓嶆槸鎵ц鍏ㄩ儴姝ラ涔熶笉鏄崟鐙墽琛屾楠?锛屽崟鐙€夋嫨浜嗗叾浠栨楠ゆ椂鎵嶆墽琛?
        if not is_pipeline and choice != "0" and should_run_step(0, choice, is_pipeline=False):
            success, _, _ = run_step(
                0, "娓呯悊杈撳嚭鐩綍JSON鏂囦欢", step0_clean_json, None, config, timer, audio_clipper,
                enabled=True
            )
            if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
                console.print("[error]娓呯悊JSON鏂囦欢澶辫触锛屾牴鎹厤缃粓姝㈡祦姘寸嚎[/error]")
                logger.error("娓呯悊JSON鏂囦欢澶辫触锛屾牴鎹厤缃粓姝㈡祦姘寸嚎")
                return False
        
        # 娴佹按绾垮鐞?
        # 姝ラ1: 瑙嗛杞爜
        success, current_video, _ = run_step(
            1, "瑙嗛杞爜", step1_transcode, current_video, config, timer, audio_clipper,
            enabled=should_run_step(1, choice, is_pipeline) and config["enable_step1"]
        )
        if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
            if not is_pipeline: return False # 鍗曟鎵ц澶辫触鍒欓€€鍑?
            console.print("[error]瑙嗛杞爜澶辫触锛屾牴鎹厤缃粓姝㈡祦姘寸嚎[/error]")
            logger.error("瑙嗛杞爜澶辫触锛屾牴鎹厤缃粓姝㈡祦姘寸嚎")
            return False
        if not is_pipeline and choice == "1": return True # 鍗曟鎵ц鎴愬姛鍒欓€€鍑?
            
        # 姝ラ2: 鍓緫姘斿彛
        success, current_video, _ = run_step(
            2, "鍓緫姘斿彛", step2_remove_silence, current_video, config, timer, audio_clipper,
            enabled=should_run_step(2, choice, is_pipeline) and config["enable_step2"]
        )
        if not success and config["stop_on_error"]:
            if not is_pipeline: return False
            console.print("[error]鍓緫姘斿彛澶辫触锛屾牴鎹厤缃粓姝㈡祦姘寸嚎[/error]")
            logger.error("鍓緫姘斿彛澶辫触锛屾牴鎹厤缃粓姝㈡祦姘寸嚎")
            return False
        if not is_pipeline and choice == "2": return True
            
        # 姝ラ3: 瑙嗛淇
        success, current_video, _ = run_step(

    parser = _build_parser()
    args = parser.parse_args(argv)
    return _run_pipeline_with_args(args)

from __future__ import annotations

import multiprocessing
import os
from concurrent.futures import ProcessPoolExecutor
from concurrent.futures.process import BrokenProcessPool
from pathlib import Path
from threading import RLock
from typing import Any, Dict, Optional


def _reconfigure_stdio_utf8() -> None:
    for stream_name in ("stdout", "stderr"):
        stream = getattr(os.sys, stream_name, None)
        if stream is None:
            continue
        reconfigure = getattr(stream, "reconfigure", None)
        if callable(reconfigure):
            try:
                reconfigure(encoding="utf-8", errors="replace")
            except Exception:
                continue


def _apply_env(overrides: Optional[Dict[str, str]]) -> Dict[str, Optional[str]]:
    snapshot: Dict[str, Optional[str]] = {}
    for key, value in (overrides or {}).items():
        snapshot[key] = os.environ.get(key)
        if value:
            os.environ[key] = str(value)
        elif key in os.environ:
            os.environ.pop(key, None)
    return snapshot


def _restore_env(snapshot: Dict[str, Optional[str]]) -> None:
    for key, value in snapshot.items():
        if value is None:
            os.environ.pop(key, None)
        else:
            os.environ[key] = value


def _set_repo_root(repo_root: str) -> str:
    resolved = str(Path(repo_root).resolve())
    if resolved not in os.sys.path:
        os.sys.path.insert(0, resolved)
    os.chdir(resolved)
    return resolved


def _child_initializer(repo_root: str, base_env: Optional[Dict[str, str]]) -> None:
    _reconfigure_stdio_utf8()
    _apply_env(base_env)
    _set_repo_root(repo_root)


def _warmup_job(payload: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    _reconfigure_stdio_utf8()
    _set_repo_root(str(payload["repo_root"]))
    env_snapshot = _apply_env(payload.get("env"))
    try:
        from domain.video.pre.main import pipeline as pipeline_module

        warmed = pipeline_module.warm_pipeline_runtime(output_dir=str(payload["output_dir"]))
        return {"warmed": bool(warmed)}
    finally:
        _restore_env(env_snapshot)


def _execute_pipeline_job(payload: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    _reconfigure_stdio_utf8()
    _set_repo_root(str(payload["repo_root"]))
    env_snapshot = _apply_env(payload.get("env"))
    try:
        from domain.video.pre.main import pipeline as pipeline_module

        success = pipeline_module.run_pipeline_request(
            input_path=str(payload["input_path"]),
            output_dir=str(payload["output_dir"]),
            model=payload.get("model"),
            file_encoding=payload.get("file_encoding"),
            enable_preprocess=bool(payload.get("enable_preprocess", False)),
            disable_preprocess=bool(payload.get("disable_preprocess", False)),
            clip_text=payload.get("clip_text"),
            clip_text_file=payload.get("clip_text_file"),
            forum_post_info_json=payload.get("forum_post_info_json"),
            organize_delete_original=payload.get("organize_delete_original"),
        )
        if not success:
            raise RuntimeError("warm internal pipeline returned False")
        return {"success": True}
    finally:
        _restore_env(env_snapshot)


class InternalPipelineWarmRunner:
    def __init__(
        self,
        *,
        repo_root: str,
        output_dir: str,
        pool_size: int = 1,
        warmup_on_start: bool = True,
        base_env: Optional[Dict[str, str]] = None,
        logger: Any = None,
    ) -> None:
        self.repo_root = str(Path(repo_root).resolve())
        self.output_dir = str(Path(output_dir).resolve())
        self.pool_size = max(1, int(pool_size))
        self.warmup_on_start = bool(warmup_on_start)
        self.base_env = dict(base_env or {})
        self.logger = logger
        self._executor: Optional[ProcessPoolExecutor] = None
        self._lock = RLock()

    def start(self) -> None:
        with self._lock:
            if self._executor is not None:
                return
            context = multiprocessing.get_context("spawn")
            self._executor = ProcessPoolExecutor(
                max_workers=self.pool_size,
                mp_context=context,
                initializer=_child_initializer,
                initargs=(self.repo_root, self.base_env),
            )
            if self.warmup_on_start:
                for _ in range(self.pool_size):
                    self._executor.submit(
                        _warmup_job,
                        {
                            "repo_root": self.repo_root,
                            "output_dir": self.output_dir,
                            "env": {},
                        },
                    )
            if self.logger is not None:
                self.logger.info(
                    "internal warm runner started: pool_size=%s warmup_on_start=%s",
                    self.pool_size,
                    self.warmup_on_start,
                )

    def stop(self) -> None:
        with self._lock:
            executor = self._executor
            self._executor = None
        if executor is not None:
            executor.shutdown(wait=False, cancel_futures=True)
            if self.logger is not None:
                self.logger.info("internal warm runner stopped")

    def execute(self, *, payload: Dict[str, Any], timeout_seconds: int) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        if self._executor is None:
            self.start()
        executor = self._executor
        if executor is None:
            raise RuntimeError("warm runner executor unavailable")

        try:
            future = executor.submit(_execute_pipeline_job, payload)
            return future.result(timeout=timeout_seconds)
        except BrokenProcessPool as exc:
            self.stop()
            raise RuntimeError(f"warm runner process pool broke: {exc}") from exc

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass
import importlib
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional
import json
import uuid

try:
    run_stage4_asr = importlib.import_module("domain.video.stages.stage4_asr").run
    run_stage6_5_resub = importlib.import_module("domain.video.stages.stage6_5_resub").run
    run_stage6_clip = importlib.import_module("domain.video.stages.stage6_clip").run
    stage_artifact_path = importlib.import_module("domain.video.stages.utils").stage_artifact_path
except Exception:  # pragma: no cover - exercised only when legacy modules are absent.
    @dataclass
    class _StageResult:
        success: bool
        output_file: Optional[str] = None
        error_message: Optional[str] = None

    def stage_artifact_path(output_dir: str, task_id: str, stage_name: str, suffix: str) -> Path:
        stage_dir = Path(output_dir) / task_id / "_stages"
        stage_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
        return stage_dir / f"{task_id}_{stage_name}{suffix}"

    def _missing_stage(*_args, **_kwargs) -> _StageResult:
        return _StageResult(success=False, error_message="legacy stage module unavailable")

    run_stage4_asr = _missing_stage
    run_stage6_clip = _missing_stage
    run_stage6_5_resub = _missing_stage


@dataclass
class GradioBackendConfig:
    output_dir: str = "output/gradio"


class GradioBackend:
    def __init__(self, config: GradioBackendConfig | None = None) -> None:
        self.config = config or GradioBackendConfig()
        Path(self.config.output_dir).mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

    def run_asr(
        self,
        input_video: str,
        *,
        hotwords: str = "",
        speaker: str = "",
        task_id: str | None = None,
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        source = self._resolve_local_video(input_video)
        if source is None:
            return {"success": False, "error": "input video not found"}

        resolved_task_id = task_id or self._new_task_id("asr")
        hotword_list = self._parse_csv_text(hotwords)
        forum_info = {"hotwords": hotword_list}
        if speaker.strip():
            forum_info["speaker"] = speaker.strip()

        result = run_stage4_asr(
            input_video=str(source),
            output_dir=self.config.output_dir,
            task_id=resolved_task_id,
            forum_post_info=forum_info,
            hotwords=hotword_list,
            speaker=speaker.strip() or None,
        )
        if not result.success:
            return {
                "success": False,
                "task_id": resolved_task_id,
                "error": result.error_message or "stage4_asr failed",
            }

        manifest = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage4_asr_manifest", ".json")
        transcript = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage4_asr_transcript", ".txt")
        subtitles = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage4_asr_subtitles", ".srt")
        return {
            "success": True,
            "task_id": resolved_task_id,
            "output_video": result.output_file,
            "manifest_path": str(manifest),
            "transcript_path": str(transcript),
            "subtitle_path": str(subtitles),
        }

    def run_clip(
        self,
        input_video: str,
        *,
        clip_text: str = "",
        speaker: str = "",
        task_id: str | None = None,
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        source = self._resolve_local_video(input_video)
        if source is None:
            return {"success": False, "error": "input video not found"}

        resolved_task_id = task_id or self._new_task_id("clip")
        if clip_text.strip():
            script = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage5_ai_script", ".txt")
            script.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
            script.write_text(clip_text.strip() + "\n", encoding="utf-8")

        if speaker.strip():
            stage4_manifest = stage_artifact_path(
                self.config.output_dir,
                resolved_task_id,
                "stage4_asr_manifest",
                ".json",
            )
            stage4_manifest.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
            stage4_manifest.write_text(
                json.dumps({"task_id": resolved_task_id, "speaker": speaker.strip()}, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2),
                encoding="utf-8",
            )

        result = run_stage6_clip(
            input_video=str(source),
            output_dir=self.config.output_dir,
            task_id=resolved_task_id,
        )
        if not result.success:
            return {
                "success": False,
                "task_id": resolved_task_id,
                "error": result.error_message or "stage6_clip failed",
            }

        manifest = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage6_clip_manifest", ".json")
        return {
            "success": True,
            "task_id": resolved_task_id,
            "output_video": result.output_file,
            "manifest_path": str(manifest),
        }

    def run_subtitle(
        self,
        input_video: str,
        *,
        task_id: str | None = None,
        subtitle_format: str = "ass",
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        source = self._resolve_local_video(input_video)
        if source is None:
            return {"success": False, "error": "input video not found"}

        resolved_task_id = task_id or self._new_task_id("sub")
        result = run_stage6_5_resub(
            input_video=str(source),
            output_dir=self.config.output_dir,
            task_id=resolved_task_id,
        )
        if not result.success:
            return {
                "success": False,
                "task_id": resolved_task_id,
                "error": result.error_message or "stage6_5_resub failed",
            }

        srt_path = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage6_5_resub_subtitles", ".srt")
        ass_path = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage6_5_resub_subtitles", ".ass")
        manifest = stage_artifact_path(self.config.output_dir, resolved_task_id, "stage6_5_resub_manifest", ".json")

        preferred = ass_path if subtitle_format.strip().lower() == "ass" else srt_path
        return {
            "success": True,
            "task_id": resolved_task_id,
            "output_video": result.output_file,
            "subtitle_path": str(preferred),
            "subtitle_srt": str(srt_path),
            "subtitle_ass": str(ass_path),
            "manifest_path": str(manifest),
        }

    def run_manual_chain(
        self,
        input_video: str,
        *,
        hotwords: str = "",
        clip_text: str = "",
        speaker: str = "",
        subtitle_format: str = "ass",
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        task_id = self._new_task_id("manual")
        asr_result = self.run_asr(input_video, hotwords=hotwords, speaker=speaker, task_id=task_id)
        if not asr_result.get("success"):
            return {"success": False, "stage": "asr", "error": asr_result.get("error")}

        clip_result = self.run_clip(input_video, clip_text=clip_text, speaker=speaker, task_id=task_id)
        if not clip_result.get("success"):
            return {"success": False, "stage": "clip", "error": clip_result.get("error")}

        subtitle_result = self.run_subtitle(
            clip_result.get("output_video") or input_video,
            task_id=task_id,
            subtitle_format=subtitle_format,
        )
        if not subtitle_result.get("success"):
            return {"success": False, "stage": "subtitle", "error": subtitle_result.get("error")}

        return {
            "success": True,
            "task_id": task_id,
            "asr": asr_result,
            "clip": clip_result,
            "subtitle": subtitle_result,
        }

    def _resolve_local_video(self, raw_path: str) -> Optional[Path]:
        path = Path(str(raw_path or "").strip())
        if not path.exists() or not path.is_file():
            return None
        return path

    def _new_task_id(self, prefix: str) -> str:
        return f"gradio-{prefix}-{uuid.uuid4().hex[:8]}"

    def _parse_csv_text(self, raw: str) -> List[str]:
        values: List[str] = []
        for item in str(raw or "").replace("\uFF0C", ",").split(","):
            text = item.strip()
            if not text:
                continue
            if text.lower() in {value.lower() for value in values}:
                continue
            values.append(text)
        return values

    def _attach_video_render_manifest(self, task: UnifiedTask, result: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        normalized_result = dict(result or {})
        artifacts = self._collect_video_artifacts(task=task, result=normalized_result)
        if not artifacts:
            return normalized_result

        render_manifest = self._build_video_render_manifest(
            task=task,
            result=normalized_result,
            artifacts=artifacts,
        )
        normalized_result["artifacts"] = artifacts
        normalized_result["render_manifest"] = render_manifest
        return normalized_result

    def _collect_video_artifacts(self, task: UnifiedTask, result: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        task_dir = Path(self.config.output_dir) / task.task_id
        output_path = str(result.get("output_path") or "").strip()
        named_output_path = str(result.get("named_output_path") or "").strip()
        original_output_path = str(result.get("original_output_path") or "").strip()
        preferred_primary_path = output_path or named_output_path or original_output_path
        primary_resolved = self._safe_resolve_existing_path(preferred_primary_path)

        candidate_files: Dict[str, Path] = {}
        for raw_path in (output_path, named_output_path, original_output_path):
            resolved = self._safe_resolve_existing_path(raw_path)
            if resolved is not None:
                candidate_files[str(resolved)] = resolved

        candidate_dirs: List[Path] = []
        for raw_dir in (
            str(task_dir),
            str(Path(output_path).parent) if output_path else "",
            str(Path(named_output_path).parent) if named_output_path else "",
            str(Path(original_output_path).parent) if original_output_path else "",
        ):
            resolved_dir = self._safe_resolve_existing_dir(raw_dir)
            if resolved_dir is None:
                continue
            if resolved_dir not in candidate_dirs:
                candidate_dirs.append(resolved_dir)

        for base_dir in candidate_dirs:
            try:
                files = sorted(
                    [path for path in base_dir.rglob("*") if path.is_file()],
                    key=lambda item: str(item).lower(),
                )
            except Exception:
                continue
            for path in files:
                if not self._should_expose_video_artifact(path):
                    continue
                resolved = self._safe_resolve_existing_path(str(path))
                if resolved is None:
                    continue
                candidate_files[str(resolved)] = resolved

        artifacts: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
        used_ids: set[str] = set()
        task_dir_resolved = self._safe_resolve_existing_dir(str(task_dir))
        sorted_files = sorted(
            candidate_files.values(),
            key=lambda item: self._video_artifact_sort_key(
                path=item,
                primary_resolved=primary_resolved,
            ),
        )
        single_artifact_roles = {
            "final_video",
            "video_subtitled",
            "video_no_subtitle",
            "coverless_video",
            "subtitle_srt",
            "subtitle_ass",
            "transcript_text",
            "clip_text",
            "forum_post_info",
            "cover_image",
            "cover_manifest",
            "processing_log",
            "pipeline_state",
            "video",
        }
        selected_files: List[Tuple[Path, str, str]] = []
        seen_roles: set[str] = set()
        for path in sorted_files:
            role, kind = self._classify_video_artifact_role(
                path=path,
                primary_resolved=primary_resolved,
            )
            if role in single_artifact_roles and role in seen_roles:
                continue
            seen_roles.add(role)
            selected_files.append((path, role, kind))

        for index, artifact_info in enumerate(selected_files, start=1):
            path, role, kind = artifact_info
            artifact_id = self._build_video_artifact_id(
                role=role,
                index=index,
                used_ids=used_ids,
            )
            relative_path = self._build_artifact_relative_path(path=path, task_dir=task_dir_resolved)
            stat = path.stat()
            artifacts.append(
                {
                    "artifact_id": artifact_id,
                    "kind": kind,
                    "role": role,
                    "filename": path.name,
                    "path": str(path),
                    "relative_path": relative_path,
                    "size_bytes": int(stat.st_size),
                    "is_primary": primary_resolved is not None and path == primary_resolved,
                }
            )
        return artifacts

    def _build_video_render_manifest(
        self,
        task: UnifiedTask,
        result: Dict[str, Any],
        artifacts: List[Dict[str, Any]],
    ) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        primary_artifact_id = ""
        videos: Dict[str, str] = {}
        subtitles: Dict[str, str] = {}
        texts: Dict[str, str] = {}
        context: Dict[str, str] = {}
        logs: Dict[str, str] = {}
        cover: Dict[str, str] = {}
        pipeline_state: Dict[str, Any] = {}

        for artifact in artifacts:
            artifact_id = str(artifact.get("artifact_id") or "").strip()
            role = str(artifact.get("role") or "").strip()
            path_text = str(artifact.get("path") or "").strip()
            if artifact.get("is_primary") and artifact_id:
                primary_artifact_id = artifact_id

            if role == "final_video" and artifact_id:
                videos["primary"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "video_subtitled" and artifact_id and "subtitled" not in videos:
                videos["subtitled"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "video_no_subtitle" and artifact_id:
                videos["no_subtitle"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "coverless_video" and artifact_id:
                videos["coverless"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "video" and artifact_id and "alternate" not in videos:
                videos["alternate"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "subtitle_srt" and artifact_id:
                subtitles["srt"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "subtitle_ass" and artifact_id:
                subtitles["ass"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "transcript_text" and artifact_id:
                subtitles["script"] = artifact_id
                texts["script"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "clip_text" and artifact_id:
                texts["clip_text"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "forum_post_info" and artifact_id:
                context["forum_post_info"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "cover_image" and artifact_id and "image" not in cover:
                cover["image"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "cover_manifest" and artifact_id:
                cover["manifest"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "processing_log" and artifact_id and "processing" not in logs:
                logs["processing"] = artifact_id
            elif role == "pipeline_state" and artifact_id:
                pipeline_state = {
                    "artifact_id": artifact_id,
                    "path": path_text,
                }
                pipeline_state.update(self._read_pipeline_state_summary(path_text))

        manifest: Dict[str, Any] = {
            "task_id": task.task_id,
            "artifact_count": len(artifacts),
            "primary_artifact_id": primary_artifact_id,
            "primary_output_path": str(result.get("output_path") or "").strip(),
            "videos": videos,
            "subtitles": subtitles,
            "cover": cover,
        }
        if texts:
            manifest["texts"] = texts
        if context:
            manifest["context"] = context
        if logs:
            manifest["logs"] = logs
        if pipeline_state:
            manifest["pipeline_state"] = pipeline_state
        return manifest

    def _safe_resolve_existing_path(self, value: str) -> Optional[Path]:
        text = str(value or "").strip()
        if not text:
            return None
        candidate = Path(text)
        if not candidate.exists() or not candidate.is_file():
            return None
        try:
            return candidate.resolve()
        except Exception:
            return candidate

    def _safe_resolve_existing_dir(self, value: str) -> Optional[Path]:
        text = str(value or "").strip()
        if not text:
            return None
        candidate = Path(text)
        if not candidate.exists() or not candidate.is_dir():
            return None
        try:
            return candidate.resolve()
        except Exception:
            return candidate

    def _should_expose_video_artifact(self, path: Path) -> bool:
        suffix = path.suffix.lower()
        name = path.name.lower()
        video_exts = {".mp4", ".mov", ".mkv", ".avi", ".m4v", ".webm"}
        image_exts = {".png", ".jpg", ".jpeg", ".webp"}
        if suffix in video_exts or suffix in image_exts:
            return True
        if name in {"total.srt", "total.ass", "script.txt", "state.json"}:
            return True
        if name in {"clip_text.txt", "forum_post_info.json"}:
            return True
        if suffix == ".json" and "cover_manifest" in name:
            return True
        if suffix == ".log":
            return True
        return False

    def _classify_video_artifact_role(self, path: Path, primary_resolved: Optional[Path]) -> Tuple[str, str]:
        text = path.name.lower()
        suffix = path.suffix.lower()
        if primary_resolved is not None and path == primary_resolved:
            return "final_video", "video"
        if text == "total.srt":
            return "subtitle_srt", "subtitle"
        if text == "total.ass":
            return "subtitle_ass", "subtitle"
        if text == "script.txt":
            return "transcript_text", "transcript"
        if text == "clip_text.txt":
            return "clip_text", "text"
        if text == "forum_post_info.json":
            return "forum_post_info", "context"
        if text == "state.json":
            return "pipeline_state", "manifest"
        if suffix == ".json" and "cover_manifest" in text:
            return "cover_manifest", "manifest"
        if suffix == ".log":
            return "processing_log", "log"
        if suffix in {".png", ".jpg", ".jpeg", ".webp"}:
            return "cover_image", "image"
        if "鏃犲皝闈㈡枃瀛楀彲鑷敱娣诲姞" in path.name:
            return "coverless_video", "video"
        if "鏃犲瓧骞曠増" in path.name:
            return "video_no_subtitle", "video"
        if "甯﹀瓧骞曠増" in path.name:
            return "video_subtitled", "video"
        return "video", "video"

    def _video_artifact_sort_key(self, path: Path, primary_resolved: Optional[Path]) -> Tuple[int, str]:
        role, _ = self._classify_video_artifact_role(path=path, primary_resolved=primary_resolved)
        order = {
            "final_video": 0,
            "video_subtitled": 1,
            "video_no_subtitle": 2,
            "coverless_video": 3,
            "subtitle_srt": 4,
            "subtitle_ass": 5,
            "transcript_text": 6,
            "clip_text": 7,
            "forum_post_info": 8,
            "cover_image": 9,
            "cover_manifest": 10,
            "processing_log": 11,
            "pipeline_state": 12,
            "video": 13,
        }
        return (order.get(role, 99), str(path).lower())

    def _build_video_artifact_id(self, role: str, index: int, used_ids: set[str]) -> str:
        base = re.sub(r"[^a-z0-9]+", "_", str(role or "artifact").lower()).strip("_") or "artifact"
        candidate = base
        if candidate in used_ids:
            candidate = f"{base}_{index}"
        used_ids.add(candidate)
        return candidate

    def _build_artifact_relative_path(self, path: Path, task_dir: Optional[Path]) -> str:
        if task_dir is None:
            return path.name
        try:
            return str(path.relative_to(task_dir))
        except Exception:
            return path.name

    def _read_pipeline_state_summary(self, state_path: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        path = self._safe_resolve_existing_path(state_path)
        if path is None:
            return {}
        try:
            payload = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
        except Exception:
            return {}
        if not isinstance(payload, dict):
            return {}
        summary: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        if "last_completed_step" in payload:
            try:
                summary["last_completed_step"] = int(payload.get("last_completed_step"))
            except Exception:
                pass
        step_name = str(payload.get("last_completed_step_name") or payload.get("step_name") or "").strip()
        if step_name:
            summary["last_completed_step_name"] = step_name
        output_file = str(payload.get("output_file") or "").strip()
        if output_file:
            summary["output_file"] = output_file
        return summary

    def _is_final_output_already_equivalent(self, output_path: str, original_filename: str) -> bool:
        output_file = Path(str(output_path or "").strip())
        output_name = output_file.name
        if not output_name:
            return False
        parsed = Path(self._sanitize_filename(original_filename))
        stem = parsed.stem if parsed.suffix else parsed.name
        if not stem:
            return False
        suffix = parsed.suffix or output_file.suffix or ".mp4"
        expected = f"{stem}_final{suffix}"
        return output_name.lower() == expected.lower()
